Welsh AMs ta damu game da 'yadda ake zama kamar wawaye'
Akwai tsoron haɗari a tsakanin wasu AMs a bisa shawarar canza muƙaminsu zuwa MWPs (Mamban Majalisar Dokoki ta Welsh).
Abin ya tashi ne saboda shirye-shirye na canza sunan taron zuwa Majalisar Dokoki ta Welsh.
AM a ɓangaren siyasa sun damu ƙwarai don zai iya haifar da ba’a.
Wani AM na Jam’iyyar Labour ya ce ƙungiyar ta damu "yana rauji da Twp da kuma Pwp."
Don masu karatu a wajen Wales: A cikin Welsh twp yana nufin hauka kuma pwp yana nufin kashi.
Wani Plaid AM ya ce gungun gaba ɗaya “ba su ji daɗi ba” kuma ya ba da shawarar zaɓuɓɓuka.
Wani mai ra’ayin riƙau na Welsh ya ce gungun “ba shi da wani abu a zuciya” game da canza sunan, amma ya lura wani ɗan gajeren bayani ne daga MWP zuwa Muppet.
A wannan bigiren, ana furta harafin w na Welsh ne kwatankwacin furucin Turanci na Yorshire na harafin u.
Hukumar Majalisar, wanda a yanzu haka ke rubuta daftarin dokar don gabatar da canje-canjen sunan, ta ce:  “Hukuncin ƙarshe a kan kowaɗanne abubuwa masu bayyanarwa abin da ake kiran mambobi na Majalisar zai kasance kuwa wani batu ne don mambobin da kansu.”
Dokar Gwamnatin Welsh ta 2017 ta ba wa majalisar Welsh iko na canza sunanta.
A cikin Yuni, Hukumar ta wallafa sakamako na wata tattaunawar jama’a a kan ƙudurorin wadanda suka sami babban goyon baya don kiran majalisar Majalisar Dokokin Welsh.
A kan batun sunan AMs ɗin, Hukumar ta fi son Mambobin Majalisar Dokokin Welsh ko WMPs, amma zaɓin MWP ya sami mafi goyon bayan a cikin wata tattaunawar jama’a.
A fili AMs suna ba da shawarar wasu zaɓuɓɓuka ne, amma gwagwarmayar isa ga matsaya za ta iya zama mai wahala ga Jami’i Mai Kula, Elin Jones, wanda ake tsammanin za ta mila daftarin dokar a kan canje-canje a cikin makonni.
Dokar a kan canje-canjen za su haɗa da sauran canje-canje na yadda majalisar ke aiki, da ya haɗa da ƙa’idoji a kan ayyana rashin cancanta na AMs da kuma tsara tsari na kwamitin.
AMs za su sami kaɗa kuri’ar karshe a kan batun abin da za a kira su da shi a yayin da suka yi mahawarar dokar.
‘Yan Macedonia sun tafi yin zaɓuɓɓuka a cikin zaɓen raba gardama a kan canza sunan kasar
Masu kada kuri’a za su yi zaɓe a kan ko su canza sunan kasarsu zuwa “Jamhuriyyar Macedonia ta Arewa.”
An saita sanannen zaɓen ne don wani ƙoƙari na warware wani rikicin da ya yi shekara da shekara tare da makwaɓciyar ƙasa ta Greece, wadda ke da lardinta da ake kira Macedonia.
Athens ta jima tana jajircewa cewa sunan makwaɓciyarta daga arewaci yana wakiltar wani ƙorafi ne a kan yankinta kuma ta sha maimaita ƙin neman matsayin mamba a Tarayyar Turai da Ƙungiyar Ƙawance ta NATO.
Shugaban Ƙasar Macedonia Gjorge Ivanov, wani mai adawa da tsarin zaɓen kai tsaye a kan canza sunan, ya ce zai yi watsi da zaɓen.
Amma, masu goyon bayan zaɓen raba gardamar, da suka haɗa da Firaminista Zoran Zaev, suna mahawara cewa canza sunan wani ɗan aiki ne da dole a yi don a shiga Tarayyar Turai da Ƙungiyar Ƙawance ta NATO.
Ƙararrawar St. Martin's Sun yi Shiru Saboda Majami’u a cikin Harlem suna cikin Gwargwarmaya
“A tarihi, tsofaffin mutanen da na yi magana da su sun ce akwai wata mashaya da wata majami’a a kowace kusurwa,” Inji Mista Adams.
“A yau kuwa, babu ko ɗaya.”
Ya ce ɓacewa ta mashayun abu ne na fahimta.
“Mutane suna shaƙatawa ta wata hanya daban” a ranakun nan, injin shi.
“Mashayu yanzu ba ɗakuna ne da ke makwaɓta ba inda mutane ke zuwa a-kai-a-kai.”
A game da majami’un, ya damu cewa kuɗin da ake samu daga sayar da kadarori ba za su jima idan kamar yadda shugabanni ke tsammani ba, “kuma nan ba da jimawa ba ko daga baya za su dawo idan suka fara.”
Ya ƙara da cewa, za a musanya majami’u da gine-ginen gidaje tare da manyan wurarene masu cike da irin mutane waɗanda ba za su taimaka ga sauran wuraren samun mafaka na makwaɓta.
“Mafi yawan mutane da za su sayi manyan wurare a cikin waɗannan gine-ginen za su kasance farar fata ne,” inji shi, “don haka kuwa za su gaggauta ranar da za a ce waɗannan majami’u sun rufe gaba ɗaya saboda akwai yiwuwar mafi yawanci waɗannan mutane da suka motsa cikin wadannan manyan wuraren su zama mambobi na waɗannan majami’u.”
Duka majami’un guda biyu farar fata ne suka gina su kafin Harlem ta zama alƙaryar baƙaƙen fata - Al’ummar da ke Alƙaryar a 1870, shekaru goma bayan St. Martin’s.
Asalin farar fata mahalarta ‘yan Methodist sun fita ne a cikin shekaru na 1930.
Wani taron masu ibada baƙaƙe da ke yin ibada a kusa suka mallaki ginin.
Taron baƙaƙen fata masu ibada ne suka karɓe ragamar St. Martin’s a ƙarƙashin Rabaran John Howard Johnson, wanda ya jagoranci ‘yan kasuwa da su ƙaurace ma sayen kaya a kan layi na 125, wani babban layin yin sayayya a Harlem, wanda ya jajirce a wajen yin hayar ma’aikata ko tallafawa baƙaƙen fata.
Wata gobara a cikin 1939 ta lalata ginin sosai, amma kamar yadda mabiyan Fada Johnson suka yi shirye-shirye na sake ginin, su ne suka buɗe kayan kiɗan majami’ar.
Rabaran David Johnson, dan Fada Johnson da wanda ya gaje shi a St. Martin's, a cikin alfahari ya kiran kayan kiɗan majami’ar “ƙararrawowin mutane talakawa.”
Ƙwararren da ya kaɗa ƙararrawar a watan Yuli ya kira shi da wani abu daban: “Wata ajiyayyar dukiyar al’ada” da “wani kayan tarihi da ba za a iya maida gurbinsa ba.”
Kwararren, Tiffany Ng na Jami’ar Michigan, har ila yau ya lura cewa shi ne kayan kiɗa na farko a duniya da wani mawaki baƙar fata ya rera, wato Dionisio A. Lind, wanda ya motsa babban kayan kiɗan a Majami’ar Riverside shekaru 18 da suka wuce.
Mista Merriweather ya ce St. Martin's ɗin ba ta musanya shi ba.
Abin da ya bayyana a St. Martin’s a ‘yan watanni da suka wuce ya zama wani labari mai ruɗarwa na masana zane da ‘yan kwangila, wasu da shugabannin majami’ar da ba su da ilimi suka kawo, sauran kuwa daga ikon babban limamin ‘yan Episcopal.
Sai kwamitin vestry ɗin - hukumar gudanar da yankin iyakar majami’ar, da ta haɗa da shugabanni da ba su da ilimi - sun rubuta wa babban limamin a Yuli da damuwowinsu cewa yankin iyakar majami’ar “zai nemi mika kuɗaɗen da aka kashe” zuwa kwamitin vestry ɗin, duk da cewa ba a sa kwamitin vestry ɗin ba a yin hayar masu zanen da ‘yan kwangilar da yankin iyakar majami’ar suka sa ba.
Wasu mabiya sun yi ƙorafi game da rashin bayyana abin da aka yi ta ɓangaren yankin iyakar majami’ar.
Babban kifin teku ya raunata mai iyon neman lobster ɗan shekaru 13 a California
Wani babban kifin teku ya kai hari da raunata wani yaro mai shekaru 13 a ranar Asabar a lokacin da yake iyon neman losbter a cikin California a ranar buɗe lokacin lobster, kamar yadda jami’ai suka ce.
Harin ya faru ne kawai kafin ƙarfe 7 na safe kusa da Bakin Tekun Beacon a cikin Encinitas.
Chad Hammel ya fada wa gidan talabijin na KSWB-TV a San Diego yana iyo ne tare da abokansa na kusan rabin sa’a a ranar Asabar da safe a lokacin da ya ji yaron yana kururuwa shi ke nan sai ya nufi wurin tare da wani gungun mutane don su jawo shi waje daga ruwan.
Hammel ya ce da farko ya ɗauka wata annishuwa ce ta kama wani losbter, amma shi ke nan sai ya “gano cewa ihu yake yi, ‘An cije ni!
An cije ni!’
An buɗe kashin kafaɗarsa gaba ɗaya,” inji Hammel da ya gani a lokacin da isa wurin yaron.
“Na yi ihu ga kowa don su fita daga ruwan. Hammel ya ƙara da cewa, ‘Akwai babban kifin teku a cikin ruwan!”
An ɗauki yaron a cikin jirgin sama zuwa Asibitin Yara na Rady da ke cikin San Diego inda aka jera shi a yanayi mai tsanani.
Ba a san irie-iren jinsunan babban kifin tekun da ya yi wannan harin ba.
Kyaftin Larry Giles mai kula da rayuwa ya ce a gaban maneman labarai cewa an ga wani babban kifin teku a cikin yankin ‘yan makonni baya, amma an ƙudurta cewa ba daga wani jinsuna ne babban kifi mai haɗari ne ba.
Giles ya kara da cewa wanda abin da ya shafa ya ji raunuka munana a kan yankin sama na gadon bayansa.
Jami’ai sun rufe iso ga bakin tekun daga Bakin Tekun Ponto na cikin Casablad zuwa Swami's a cikin Ecinitas na sa’o’i 48 don dalilan bincike da kariya.
Giles ya lura cewa akwai fiye da jinsunan 135 na manyan kifin teku a cikin yankin, amma mafi yawa ba a ɗauka suna da haɗari.
Sainsbury’s yana shirye-shiryen shiga kasuwar kwalliya ta Birtaniyya
Sainsbury’s yana ɗaukan Boots, Superdrug da Debenhams tare da irin ɓangarorin shagon salon kwalliya da aka ɗauka masa ma’aikata da ƙwararrun masu ba da taimako.
A matsayin ɓangaren shiga cikin kasuwar kwalliya ta Birtaniyya ta Fam biliyan 2.8, wadda ke ci gaba da haɓaka duk da cewa cinikayyar ado da kayan gida ta sami koma baya, za a gwada manyan ɓangarorin kwalliya a shaguna 11 na kasar kuma a ɗauke su zuwa ƙarin shaguna a shekara mai zuwa idan abin ya ci wata nasara.
Zuba jari a harkar kwalliya yana zuwa ne kamar yadda manyan shagunan sayar da kaya ke fafutukar hanyoyi don yin amfani da gurbin da babu kome da a da na ajiye talabijoji ne, da na’urorin dafa abinci da kayan gida.
Sainsbury’s ya ce zai ruɓanya girma na abubuwan da zai samar na kwalliya har kusan kayayyaki 3,000, da suka haɗa da nau’uka kamar su Revlon, Essie, Tweezerman da Dokta PawPaw a lokaci na farko.
Ranji-ranji da ke nan daga L'Oreal, Maybelline da Burt's Bees su ma za su sami gurbi masu yankin nau’uka iri ɗaya da waɗanda ake samu a cikin shaguna kamar Boots.
Haka kuma babban shagon zai sake ƙaddamar da ranjinsa na kayan zamani saboda mafi yawancin kayayyakin su zama na abotar vegan - wani abin da ke samun ƙaruwar buƙata ga kananan masu yin ciniki.
Kari a kan haka, mai sarin turare wato Shagon Turare zai gwada samar da rangwame a cikin shagunan Sainsbury's guda biyu, na farkonsu wanda ya buɗe a cikin Croydon, kudancin Landan, makon da ya wuce sa’an nan na biyun zai buɗe a cikin Selly Oak, Birmingham, daga baya cikin wannan shekarar.
Sayan kaya ta yanar gizo da ‘yar matsawa zuwa sayan abinci kadan a kowace rana a shaguna masu samar da sauki na gida yana nufi ya zama dole manyan shagunan sayar da kayan su himmatu wajen jan hankalin mutane su ziyarta.
Mike Coupe, shugaban Sainsbury's, ya ce shagunan gefen za su ci gaba da zama kamar manyan shaguna masu ɓangarori kamar yadda jerin babban shagon ke ƙoƙarin gasa da masu rangwame Aldi da Lidl tare da karin ayyuka da wanda ba na abinci ba.
Sainsbury’s yana sa wuraren sayarwa na gefe na Argos a cikin ɗaruruwan shaguna haka kuma ya gabatar da wasu Habitats tun da ya saye gaba ɗaya jerinsu shekaru biyu da suka wuce, wanda yake cewa ya ƙara inganta cinikayyar kayan abinci inda kuma ya sa samun ya zama mai riba.
Ƙoƙarin da babban shagon ya yi na da a farfaɗo da ɓangarorin kwalliyar da magunguna ya ƙare babu nasara.
Sainsbury’s ya gwada wani haɗin gwiwar kasuwanci tare da Boots a farkon shekaru na 2000, amma haɗuwar ta zo ƙarshe a bayan wani rikici na yadda za a raba kuɗaɗen da ke shigowa daga shagunan magani a cikin manyan shagunan nasa.
Sabuwar dabarar ta zo ne a bayan Sainsbury's ya sayar da kasuwancin nasa na shaguna 281 na magunguna ga  Celesio, mamallakin jerin shagunan Lloyds Pharmacy, a kuɗi Fam miliyan 125.
Ya ce Llyods zai taka wata rawa a cikin shirin, ta yin ƙarin wani ranji da aka faɗaɗa na nau’ukan kayan kula da fatar jiki na morewa da suka haɗa da La Roche-Posay da Vichy a cikin shaguna huɗu.
Paul Mills-Hicks, daraktan ciniki na Sainsbury's ya ce: “Mun canza gani da yadda ake ji na ɓangarorin kwalliya don inganta yanayi ga abokan cinikinmu.
Mun kuma zuba jari a abokan aikinmu da suka sami horarwa ta musamman waɗanda za su kasance a kusa wajen ba da shawara.
An tsara ranjinmu na nau’uka ne don dacewa da kowace buƙata kuma yanayin mai ƙayatarwa da wuraren da ke sauki wanda ke nufin wani wurin zuwa na kwalliya mai jan hankali da ke ƙalubalantar tsohuwar hanya ta sayan kaya.”
Peter Jones 'ya fusata' bayan Holly Willoughby ya fita daga kwangila ta Fam miliyan 11
Tauraron Dragons Den Peter Jones ya tafi a 'fusace' bayan mai gabatarwa a talabijin Holly Willoughby ta fita daga kwangila ta Fam miliyan 11 da irin salon nau’in rayuwarta ta kasuwanci don koma kan sababbin kwangilolinta tare da Marks da Spencer da ITV
Willoughby ba ta da lokaci na kayansu na gida da nau’in abubuwan tallafi na Truly.
An alaƙanta kasuwanin nasu ga nau’i na Gwyneth Paltrow's Goop.
Mai gabatar da shirin Wannan Safiyar, mai shekaru 37, ta je Instagram inda ta sanar za ta tafi.
Holly Willoughby ta bar Dragons" tauraron Den Peter Jones cikin fushi ya ce ta fita daga nau’in salon kasuwancinsu mai samar da kuɗi a ƙarshen lokaci - don ta fuskanci sababbin kwangilolinta masu tsoka tare da Marks & Spencer da ITV
Kafofi sun ce Jones ya ‘fusata’ ne a yayin da sananniyar yarinya talabijin ɗin ta tabbatar a lokacin wata tattaunawa mai tsauri a ranar Talata a hedikwatar babban kasuwancin nasa a cikin Marlow, Buckinghamshire, cewa sababbin kwangilolin nata - da suka kai har Fam miliyan 1.5 - na nufin yanzu ba ta da lokaci isasshe da za ta bata ga kayansu na gida da nau’in abubuwan tallafi na Truly.
An alaƙanta kasuwancin ga nau’in Gwyneth Paltrow's Goop kuma an ce zai jawo rubanyar abin da Willoughby's ke da shi da aka kimanta ya kai Fam miliyan 11.
Kamar yadda Willoughby, yar shekaru 37, ta shiga Instagram ta sanar cewa za ta bar Truly, Jones hawa jirgi ya yi ya wuce daya daga cikin gidajensa na yin hutu.
Wata kafa ta ce: “Truly shi ne a sama na abubuwan da Holly ya fifita.
Zai zama zangonta mai tsawo da zai nan gaba daga yadda za ta yi a wasu shekaru masu zuwa nan gaba.
Hukuncita da ta yanke na fitar ya sa duk waɗanda ke ciki a yanayin ban mamaki.
Ba wanda zai iya yarda da abin da ya faru a ranar Talata, ya yi kusa da ƙaddamarwar.
Akwai wani babban wuri na ajiyar kaya cike da kayayyaki a hedikwatar Marlow waɗanda an shirya sayar da su.”
Ƙwararru sun yi imani tafiyar mai gabatar da shirin na Wannan Safiyar, wadda ke cikin taurarin Birtaniyya mafi warwaso, zai jawo hasarar miliyoyi ga kamfanin saboda matsanancin zuba jari a kayayyaki daga kushin-kushin zuwa kyandira zuwa tufafi da kayan gida, da kuma yiwuwar jinkiri na ƙaddamarwar tasa.
Kuma zai ba da ma’anar ƙarshe ta wata abokanta mai tsayi.
Mahaifiyar yara uku Willoughby da mijinta Dan Baldwin sun kasance kusa da Jones da matarsa Tara Capp na shekaru goma.
Willoughby ya kafa Truly tare da Capp a cikin 2016 da Jones, mai shekaru 52, da ya shigo a matsayin shugaba a Maris.
Ma’auratan sukan yi hutu tare kuma Jones yana wani kaso 40 cikin dari a cikin kamfani talabijin mai samarwa na Baldwin.
Willoughby zai zama wani jakadan wani samfur ga M&S kuma zai maye gurbin Ant McPartlin a matsayin mai gabatar da shirin  ITV na Ni Wani Sananne Ne.
Wata kafa kusa da Jones ta ce jiya da dare “Ba za mu yi sharhi a kan al’amuransa na kasuwanci ba.”
Babbar magana ‘kuma shi ke nan sai muka fara soyayya’
Ya yi barkwanci game da sukar da zai samu daga kafafen watsa labarai don yin wani sharhi da wasu za su ɗauka “abin da bai dace da shugaban ƙasa ba” da kuma kasancewa yana ganin abu mai kyau game da shugaban Koriya ta Arewa.
Me ya sa Shugaba Trump ya ba da abubuwa masu yawa?
Trump ya ce a cikin muryarsa ta muzanta “mai yin labaran”.
“Ban barin komai.”
Ya lura cewa Kim yana da sha’awa ne a tattaunawa ta biyu bayan tattaunawarsu ta farko a Singapore a watan Yuni wanda Trump ya jinjina a matsayin wani babban mataki da ke tunkarar rage makaman nukiliya a Koriya ta Arewa.
Amma yarjejeniyoyin rage makaman nukiliyar sun ci tura.
Fiye da watanni uku bayan babban taro a cikin Singapore, babban jami’in diflomasiyyar Koriya ta Arewa Ri Yong Ho ya fada wa shugabannin duniya a Babban Taro na Majalisar Ɗinkin Duniya a ranar Asabar cewa Arewar ba ta ga wani “martani irin yadda suka yi ba” daga Amurka zuwa ga yinƙurin rage makaman da Koriya ta Arewar ta fara ba.
A maimaiko, ya lura, Amurka ta ci gaba da sa takunkumi ne da niyyar ci gaba da matsi lamba.
Trump ya ɗauki wani ra’ayi da yake jin zai yiwu a cikin jawabinsa na gangami.
“Kome yana tafiya mana daidai tare da Koriya ta Arewa,” inji shi.
“Da za mu fara yaki tare da Koriya ta Arewa.
Da an kashe miliyoyin mutane.
Yanzu kuwa muna da wannan babbar danganta.”
Ya ce ƙoƙare-ƙoƙarensa don inganta hulɗoɗi tare da Kim sun samar da sakamako mai kyau - kawowa ƙarshe gwaje-gwajen roka, taimakawa a sake mutanen da aka yi garkuwa da su da kuma samun dawowa da sauran gawawwakin sojojin Amurka gida.
Kuma ya kare hanyarsa wata iri a cikin magana mage da hulɗoɗi tare da Kim.
“Yana da sauki halayyar shugaban ƙasa, amma maimakon a sami mutane 10,000 a waje suna ƙoƙarin shigowa cikin wannan wuri mai dandazo, za mu sami kusan mutane 200 a nan wurin,” inji Trump, yana mai nuna jama’ar da ke gabansa da yatsa kai tsaye.
Tsunamin Indonesiya da Girgizar Ƙasa sun yi ɓarna a Tsibiri, Ɗaruruwa Sun Mutu
A bayan girgizar ƙasa ta Lombok, ga misali, an ce wa ƙungiyoyin ƙasashen waje da ba na gwamnati ba cewa ba a buƙatarsu.
Duk da cewa kusan fiye da kashi 10 na yawan jama’ar Lombok sun rasa matsugunansu, ba a furta hadari na kasa ba, wani sharadi da zai janyo samun taimakon kasa-da-kasa.
“A misalai da yawa, abin takaici, sun nuna a fili cewa ba sa neman taimako na ƙasa-da-ƙasa, don haka wani abu ne mai ƙan ƙalubale,” inji Misis Sumbung.
A lokacin da Save the Children ke haɗa wata ƙungiya da za ta tafi Palu, ba ta da tabbacin ko ma’aikatan ƙasashe waje za su iya aiki a ƙasa.
Mista Sutopo, mai magana da yawun hukumar haɗura ta ƙasa, ya ce jami’an Indonesiya suna auna yanayin na cikin Palu don ganin ko za a bari wakilan ƙasa-da-ƙasa su ba da gudunmawa ga ƙoƙarin tallafi.
Ganin jijjigar ƙasa da Indonesiya ta saba gani, ƙasar ta zama ta yi mummunan rashin shiryawa don bala’in rayuwa.
Duk da cewa an gina matsugunan Tsunami a cikin Aceh, ba su zama abin da ake iya gani a yankunan da ke kusa da bakin ruwa ba.
Rashin jiniyar gargarɗin tsunami da ya fito a fili a cikin Palu, duk da cewa wani gargaɗi yana aiki, zai iya yiwuwa shi ne ya ba da gudunmawa ga rasa rayuwa.
A lokuta mafiya kyau, bulaguro tsakanin tsibiran Indonesiya masu yawa yana da ƙalubale.
Haɗuran da Allah ya aiko sukan sa rabe-raben kayan buƙata ya zama da wahala sosai.
Wani asibitin jirgin ruwa da aka ajiye a cikin Lombok yana kan hanyarsa ta zuwa Palu don kula da waɗanda girgizar ƙasar ta shafa, amma zai ɗauki aƙalla kwanaki uku kafin isa wurin sabon bala’in.
Shugaba Ƙasa Joko Widodo ya maida inganta gine-ginen Indonesiya da suka lalace abin da ya sa a gaba na kamfe ɗin zaɓensa, kuma ya zuba kuɗi mai yawa a kan hanyoyi da hanyoyin jirgin ƙasa.
Amma rashin isassun kuɗaɗe ya addabi gwamnatin Mista Joko a lokacin da yake fuskantar sake zaɓe a shekara mai zuwa.
Haka kuma Mista Joko yana fuskantar matsi daga tashin-tashina bambanci addini da ya-ƙi-ci-ya-ƙi-cinyewa, inda mamobin Musulmai da suka fi rinjaye suka karɓi nau’in addini tsatstsaura.
An kashe fiye da mutane 1,000 kuma dubun-dubata sun rasa matsugunai daga gidajensu kamar yadda ‘yan daba Kirista da Musulmai ke ta yaƙi a kan tituna, suna masu yin amfani da adduna, kwari da baka, da sauran muggan makamai.
Kalli: Daniel Sturridge na Liverpool ya jawo kunnen doki da  Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge ya kare Liverpool daga wani wasa kofin ƙalubale na Premier League inda ya yi hasara ga Chelsea tare da ci a cikin mintina na 89 a ranar Asabar a Stamford Bridge a cikin Landan.
Sturridge ya karɓi wani turo ƙwallo daga Xherdan Shaqiri kusan yadina 30 a waje daga cin Chelsea tare da ‘yan ƙungiyarsa da suke biye ci 1 da 0.
Ya taɓa ƙwallon zuwa hagun ɗinsa kafin ya yi wani bugu zuwa matsaya mai nisa.
Ƙoƙarin ya ɗagu sama da akwatin inda ya gangara zuwa saman kusurwar dama na ragar.
Daga ƙarshe ƙwallon ta faɗo a saman Kepa Arrizabalaga mai tsalle inda kuma ta faɗa cikin ragar.
Sturridge ya faɗa a LiverpoolFC.com cewa “Kawai wani ƙoƙari ne na shiga wannan wurin, na samun ƙwallon kuma ‘yan wasa kamar Shaq koyaushe wasa suke yi a gaba yadda zai yiwu, don haka na yi kawai ƙoƙari ne na ƙirƙira wa kaina wani lokaci yadda zai yiwu.”
“Na ga Kante yana zuwa kuma ya taɓa sau ɗaya kuma ban yi tunani game da shi sosai ba don haka sai na yi bugun kawai.”
Chelsea ita ce a gaba da ci 1 da 0 a farkon rabin lokaci bayan ta sami wani ci a cikin minti na 25 daga tauraron Belgium Eden Hazard.
Ɗan wasa mai kai hari na Blues ya sake miƙa ƙwallo zuwa ga Mateo Kovacic a wasan, kafin ya ruga zuwa tsakiyar filin da kuma dira a cikin rabin Liverpool ɗin.
Nan da nan kuna Kovacic ya yi wata miƙawa ya ruga a tsakiyar filin.
Sa’an nan sai ya yi wani kyakkyawan buga ƙwallon, inda ya tura Hazard cikin akwatin.
Hazard ya wuce masu tsaron gida kuma ya gama zuwa matsayar raga mai nisa da sauri da wata ƙafar hagun inda ya wuce Alisson Becker na Liverpool.
Liverpool ta yi yaki da Napoli a cikin matakin gungu na Zakarun Kalubalen da karfe 3 na yamma a ranar Laraba a Stadio San Paolo da ke cikin Naples, Italiya.
Chelsea za ta kara da Videoton a cikin kofin ƙalubale na  UEFA Europa Leaguge da ƙarfe 3 na yamma a ranar Alhamis a cikin Landan.
An sami ƙarin mutuwa a tsunami na Indonesiya zuwa 832
Ƙididdigar mutuwar a girgizar ƙasar ta Indonesiyan ya haura zuwa 832, inji hukumar kula da bala’i ta ƙasar a farkon ranar Lahadi.
Abin ya ritsa da mutane masu yawa a cikin burbushin gine-gine da girgizar ƙasar mai ƙarfi na 7.5 ta rusa wadda ta auku ranar Juma’a da kuma ta jawo tashin jijiyoyin ruwa har tsawon taku 20, inji mai magana da yawun hukumar Sutopo Purwo Nugroho a lokacin da yake bayani a taron manema labarai.
Birnin Palu, mai mutane fiye da 380,000, ka kasance da ɓaraƙuzan rusassun gine-gine birjit.
‘Yan sanda sun kama mutum, mai shekaru 32, a kan tuhuma bayan kashe mata ta hanyar caka mata wuƙa
An ƙaddamar da wani bincike bayan an sami gawar wata mata a cikin Birkenhead, Merseyside wannan safiyar.
An sami mai shekaru 44 ne da karfe 7:55 na safe da raunuka na caka wuka a kan Grayson Mews da ke kan Titin John, tare da kama wani mutum mai shekaru 32 da ake tuhuma da kisan.
‘Yan sanda sun nemi mutane da ke yankin da suka gani ko kuma suka ji wani abu da su garzayo.
Sufeto Mai Bincike Brian O'Hagan ya ce: ‘Binciken yana matakan farko-farko ne amma zan yi kira ga duk wanda ke kewayen Layin John a Birkenhead wanda ya gani ko kuma ya ji wani abu da bai yarda da shi ba da ya tuntuɓe mu.
Har ila yau zan sake kira ga kowa, musamman direbobin tasi, waɗanda ƙila sun ɗauki hoto a kyamarar da ke cikin gaban mota da su tuntuɓe mu don ba mamaki ƙila suna da bayani da ke da muhimmanci ga bincikenmu.'
Wani mai magana da yawun ‘yan sanda ya tabbatar da cewa matar da aka sami gawar tata ‘yar yankin na Birkenhead ne kuma an same ta ne a cikin wani gini.
Yau da rana abokai waɗanda suka yi imani sun san matar sun je wurin da abin ya faru don yin tambayoyi game da inda aka same ta wannan safiyar.
Ana ci gaba da bincike-bincike kamar yadda ‘yan sanda suke cewa suna cikin shirin gaya wa ‘yan uwan wadda abin ya shafa.
Wani direban tasi da ke zaune a Grayson Mews ya yi ƙoƙarin ya koma cikin gidansa amma ‘yan sanda sun gaya masa cewa ba a yarda wani ya shiga ciki ko fita daga ginin ba.
Ya gagara magana a lokacin da ya gano abin da ya faru.
An gaya wa mazaunan cewa zai ɗauki sa’o’i kafin a bari su koma ciki.
An ji wani jami’in ‘yan sanda yana gaya wa wani mutum cewa ana ɗaukan gaba ɗaya wurin a matsayin wani wuri da aka aikata laifi.
Wata mata ta bayyana a wurin a tana cike da hawaye.
Ta ci gaba da maimaita ‘Abin da ban tsoro’.
Da karfe 2 na rana motoci guda biyu na ‘yan sanda sun killece tare da wata babbar mota guda kawai a waje.
Wasu jami’an sun tsaya a cikin killecewar suna duba yanki na gidajen.

Mutum-mutumi na Majalisar Dokoki ta Cromwell ta zama abin da ake tunawa na baya-bayan nan da ya faɗa ‘rikicin sake rubuta tarihi’
Kore shin zai zama sakamakon alhaki don irin salon rushe wuraren tarihi, al’ada da addini na Ingila kamar na ‘yan Taliban yadda mabiyansa masu tsatstsauran ra’ayi suka yi.
Amma Al’ummar Cromwell sun bayyana shawarar ta Mista Crick a matsayin “wauta” da “ƙoƙari na sake rubuta tarihi.”
John Goldsmith, shugaban Al’ummar Cromwell, ya ce: “Ba za a iya gujewa a cikin mahawarar da ake yi yanzu ba game da cire mutum-mutumi cewa surar Oliver Cromwell a wajen Fadar Westminster za ta zama wani abin da ake hari.
Yin hari a kan fitattun abubuwa na yaƙe-yaƙen basasar Ingila ba Cromwell na ba da oda a yi ko ya aikata ba.
Watakila abu mummunan da za a ga bayan Cromwell a kansa shi ne ayyukan da kakansa Thomas ya yi a cikin ƙarni da ya wuce.
Akwai babbar bayani game da Cromwell na Sa William Hamo Thorneycroft da ke zama hujjar ra’ayi na karni na 19 wanda kuma ɓangare na ilimin bayanan tarihin na wani sananne wanda mafi yawa suka yi imani har yanzu ya kamata a yi murna a kansa.
Mista Goldsmith ya faɗa a jaridar The Sunday Telegraph: “Mutane da yawa suna ɗaukan Cromwell, watakila sosai a shekarun karshe na karni na 19 fiye da yau, a matsayin mai kare majalisar dokoki daga matsi na waje, a cikin rikicin ba makawa da mulkin sarauta.
Ko wancan bayanin zai zama wani abu gaba ɗaya daidai ya zama batun na ci gaba da mahawara ta fuskar tarihi.
Abin da ke da tabbaci shi ne rikicin na tsakiyar ƙarni na 17 ya gyara ci gaba na ƙasarmu da aka samu daga baya, kuma Cromwell wani mutum ne sananne da aka sani wanda ke wakiltar sashe ɗaya na wancan rikicin.
Abubuwan da ya cimma a matsayin Lord Protector ya kuma kamata a yi bikinsu da tunawa da su.”
Makashi Alade ya Turmushe Manomi Dan China har Lahira
Wani alade ya kai hari da kuma kashe wani manomi a cikin wata kasuwa da ke cikin kudu-maso-yamma na China, a cewar rahotanni daga kafofin watsa labarai na gida.
An gano mutumin kawai da sunan laƙabinsa na "Yuan," wanda aka samu a mace tare da jijiyar wuya a yanke, duk jini ya rufe kusa da wani sty a kasuwar da ke cikin Liupanshui a cikin lardin Guizhou province, kamar yadda jaridar South China Morning Post ta kawo rahoto.
Wani manomin alade ya shirya yin allura ga aladu a ɗakin kiwon aladu a ranar 30 ga Mayu, 2005 a cikin Xining da Lardin Qinghai, China.
An ba da rahoton cewa ya yi bulaguro ne da ɗan uwansa daga makwaɓcin lardin Yunnan a ranar Laraba don sayar da aladu 15 a kasuwar.
Da safiyar washegari, ɗan uwan nasa ya same a mace, kuma ya ga wata ƙofa zuwa ga wani makwaɓcin wurin aladu na sty a buɗe.
Ya ce a cikin sty ɗin an sami wani babban alade namiji da jini a kan bakinsa.
Wani binciken kimiyya na abin da ya faru ya tabbatar da cewa aladen mai nauyi 550 ya murƙushe manomin har lahira, a cewar rahoton.
“Ƙafafun dan uwana sun kasance a cikin jini kuma a lanƙwashe,” ɗan uwan ya ambaci sunan laƙabinsa da “Wu” inji shi, kamar yadda Guiyang Evening News ta fada.
Bidiyo daga kyamarar tsaro ta nuna Yuan yana shiga kasuwar da ƙarfe 4:40 na safe a ranar Alhamis don ba da abinci ga aladunsa.
An sami gawarsa kusan bayan sa’a guda.
Dabbar da ta kashe mutumin ba mallakar Yuan ko ɗan uwan nasa  ba ne.
Wani manajan kasuwa ya gaya wa Evening News cewa an rufe aladen don hana shi kai hari a wani mutum daban, a lokacin da ‘yan sanda kuma ke tara bayanan hujja a wurin da abin ya faru.
An ba da rahoton cewa iyalan Yuan da hukumomin kasuwar suna tattaunawar biyan diyyar don mutuwarsa.
Ko da yake ba yawa, a da an ga misalai na harin aladu a kan ‘yan Adam.
A cikin 2016, wani alade ya kai hari ga wata mata da mijinta a gonarsu da ke Massachusetts, inda ya bar mutumin a cikin munanan raunuka.
Shekaru goma da suka wuce, wani alade mai nauyi 650 ya tsire wani manomi dan Welsh zuwa ga tantan ɗinsa har sai da matarsa ta tsoritar da dabbar ta gudu.
Bayan wani manomi mutumin Oregun aladunsa sun cinye shi a 2012, wani manomi guda ɗan Manitoba ya faɗa a CBC News cewa aladu ba su cika faɗa ba amma dandanon jini zai iya zama wani “abu da zaburar.”
“Kawai suna da wasa ne.
Su masu kamu ne, suna da son su san abu... ba su fito ne don su cutar ba.
Kawai dole ne ka mutunta su yadda ya kamata,” inji shi.
Ragowar iskar guguwar Rosa za su haifar da ruwan sama mai yawa ga kudu-maso-yamma na Amurka
Kamar yadda hasashe ya nuna, Guguwar Rosa tana samun rauni kamar yadda take motsawa ta saman ruwa mai sanyi na bakin teku na Mexico.
Amma, Rosa za ta haifar da ambaliyar ruwan sama a faɗin arewacin Mexico da kudu-maso-yamma na Amurka a kwanaki masu zuwa.
Rosa tana da iska ta mil 85 a cikin sa’a, wani Nau’i na 1 na Guguwar, a lokaci na ƙarfe 5 na safe a ranar Lahadi lokaci na Gabashi, kuma an gan ta a mil 385 na kudu-maso-yamma na Punta Eugenia, Mexico.
Ana tsammanin Rosa za ta motsa zuwa arewa a ranar Lahadi.
A lokacin da ake cikin nan, wata akalar ruwan ta fara kankama a saman Tekun Pacific inda ta motsa gabas zuwa Bakin Teku na Yamma na Amurka. Kamar yadda Rosa ke tunkaran zirin Baja California a ranar Litinin a matsayin wani babban haɗari za ta fara tura laimar zafi zuwa yankin arewaci cikin kudu-maso-yamma na Amurka.
Rosa za ta haifar da har kusan inci 10 na ruwan sama a sassan Mexico a ranar Litinin.
Sa’an nan, laimar zafin idan ta haɗu tare da akalar ruwa da ke fuskantowa za ta ƙirƙiri wani ruwan sama da zai isa wurare masu yawa a cikin kudu-maso-yamma a kwanaki masu zuwa.
A cikin gida, inci 1 zuwa 14 na ruwan sama zai haifar da mummunan ambaliya, kwararar burbushi da kuma yiwuwar zaizayar ƙasa a cikin hamadar.
Matsananciyar laimar zafi za ta iya haifar da kimomin ruwan sama da zai fuskanci incina 2 zuwa 3 a kowace sa’a a cikin wuraren, musamman a cikin sassa na kudancin Nevada da Arizona.
Ana tsammanin inci 2 zuwa 4 na ruwan sama a sassan kudu-maso-yamma, musamman a mafi yawanci na Arizona.
Akwai yiwuwar samun ambaliya ruwa ba ƙaƙƙautawa saboda yanda lalacewar yanayi ke ci gaba da ta'azzara saboda irin yadda ruwan sama ke sauka a yanki mai zafi yake jifa-jifa.
Mummunan shawara ne a fita zuwa cikin hamada da kafa ganin barazanar ruwan saman na wuri mai zafin.
Ruwan sama mai yawan zai iya haifar da kwazazzabai su zama koguna masu gudu kuma cidar ruwa za ta haifar da iska mai ƙura da kaɗa ƙura.
Akalar ruwan saman da ke fuskantowa za ta jawo ruwan sama mai yawa ta gida zuwa ga sassa na bakin teku na Kudancin California.
Akwai yiwuwar samun jimillar ruwan sama na sama da wani inci, wanda zai haifar da ɗan ƙaramin kwararar burbushi kuma hanyoyin mota su yi santsi.
Wannan zai zama ruwan sama na farko na lardin na lokacinsu na damuna.
Wani ruwan sama jifa-jifa na wurin zafi zai fara fuskantowa Arizona a makare ranar Lahadi da farkon ranar Litinin, kafin ruwan saman zai zama ya bazu da yawa ranar Litinin a makare da Talata.
Ruwan sama mai yawa zai bazu a cikin Kusurwowi Huɗu a ranar Talata har ya kai cikin Laraba.
Watan Oktoba zai iya ganin wani tsananin yanayi mai juyawa a faɗin Amurka kamar yadda Arctic ke ƙara sanyi, amma kuma wurare masu zafin za su ci gaba da kasancewa da dumi.
A wasu lokutan wannan zai kai ga canje-canje masu ban mamaki a cikin yanayi na wasu lokuta gajeru.
Akwai wani babban misali na bambance-bambancen yanayi mai ban mamaki ta cikin tsakiyar Amurka a ranar Lahadi.
Akwai kusan wani bambancin yanayi na digiri 20 tsakanin  Birnin Kansas, Missouri, da Omaha, Nebraska, da tsakanin  St. Louis da Des Moines, Iowa.
A ‘yan kwanaki masu zuwa, ɗumin lokacin zafi zai yi ƙoƙari ya ginu da sake faɗaɗa.
Ana tsammanin yawancin tsakiya da gabashin Amurka za ta ga wani ɗumi da zai fara zuwa Oktoba tare da bazuwar 80s daga Sararin Kudanci zuwa ga sassa na Arewa-maso-gabas.
Birnin New York zai iya kai wa digiri 80a ranar Talata, wanda aƙalla ya kai digiri 10 a sama matsakaici.
Hasashen yanayin namu mai tsawo yana nuna babban kintace yiwuwar matsakaicin yanayi na sama don gabashin Amurka a cikin farkon rabin Oktoba.
Fiye da mutane miliyan 20 ne suka kalli jin bahasi na Brett Kavanaugh
Fiye da mutane miliyan 20 ne suka kalli shaida mai riƙewa daga wanda aka tura sunan don kujerar Kotun Koli Brett Kavanaugh da matar da ke ƙararsa a kan cin zarafi na jima’i da ake cewa ya faru a cikin shekaru na 1980, Christine Blasey Ford, a kan hanyoyin sadarwar gidajen talabijin guda shida.
A lokacin da ake cikin haka, rikicin siyasar ya ci gaba, tare da masu yada labarai suna katsse shirin da ake yi na kullum don wani sauyi da aka yi na ranar Jumu’a a makare: wata yarjejeniya da Sanatan Arizona Jeff Flake ya haifar don Hukumar FBI ta yi wani bincike na mako guda na tuhume-tuhumen.
Ford ya faɗa a Kwamitin Shari’a na Majalisar Dattijai cewa tana da tabbaci kashi 100 cewa Kavanaugh ta cakume ta yana cikin maye kuma ya yi ƙoƙarin cire mata tufafinta a wani biki na makarantar sakandare.
Kavanaugh, a cikin shaida mai ɓacin rai, ya ce yana tabbaci kashi 100 cewa abin bai faru ba.
Ba mamaki fiye da mutane miliyan 20.4 ne a rahoton Nielsen suka kalli abin.
Kamfanin ya lasafta matsakaicin yawan masu kallo ne ta CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel da MSNBC.
Ba a sami alƙaluma ba nan da nan ga sauran hanyoyin sadarwa da suka nuna abin, da suka haɗa da PBS, C-SPAN da Fox Business Network ɗin.
Kuma Nielsen yawanci yana samun matsala ta auna mutane da suka kalla a cikin ofisoshinsu.
Don a fito da abin a fili, wancan shi ne kamar girman yawan masu kallo a wasan ƙwallo na wa ka ci ka tashiko ba da Kyaututtukan Academy.
Tashar Fox News, wadda masu gabatar da ra’ayi sun matukar goyi bayan ɗaukan na Kavanaugh, inda ya jagoranci dukkan hanyoyin sadarwa da ke da matsakaicin masu kallo miliyan 5.69 a lokacin jin bahasin da duk ranar, inji Nielsen.
ABC ita ce ta biyu mai masu kallo miliyan 3.26.
CBS tana da miliyan 3.1, NBC miliyan 2.94, MSNBC miliyan 2.89 da CNN mai miliyan 2.52, inji Nielsen.
Sha’awa ta kasance ta yi sama bayan sauraron.
Flake shi ne sananne a tsakiya a cikin diramar Juma’ar.
Bayan ofishin ‘yan Republican mai matsakaicin ra’ayi ya fitar da wata jawabi cewa zai zaɓi Kavanaugh, kyamarorin CNN da CBS sun nuna shi a ranar Jumu’a yana ihu a masu zanga-zanga a lokacin da yake ƙoƙarin hawa na’urar ɗaukan mutane zuwa saman bene zuwa ga wurin taron Kwamiti a kan Shari’a.
Ya tsaya da idanuwa a ƙasa na tsawon mintina masu yawa a yayin da ake yi masa ihu, ana nunawa a talabijin na CNN.
“Ina tsaye a nan a gabanka,” inji wata mata.
“Kana jin yana faɗan gaskiya ne ga ƙasar?
An gaya masa, “kana da dukkan ƙarfi a lokacin da mata da yawa ba su da ƙarfi.””
Flake ya ce ofishinsa ya fitar wani bayani kuma ya ce, kafin na’urar ɗaukan mutanen ta rufe, cewa yana da abu mai yawa da zai faɗa a wurin bahasin kwamitin.
Hanyoyin sadarwa na kebul da masu watsawa dukka suna yaɗa abin lokacin da ake yi sa’o’i daga baya, a lokacin da Kwamitin Shari’ar ke kaɗa kuri’a don tura ba da sunan Kavanaugh zuwa ga cikekkiyar Majalisar Dattawan don wani kaɗa kuri’ar.
Amma Flake ya ce zai yi kawai hakan ne tare da fahimtar cewa hukumar bincike ta FBI za ta duba kagen a kan wanda aka ba da sunan nasa a mako mai zuwa, wanda ‘yan tsiraru jam’iyyar Democrat suke ta fata.
Flake ya gamsu ɗan kaɗa da hirarraki tare da abokinsa, Sanatan jam’iyyar Democrat Chris Coons.
Bayan wata hira tare da Coons da sanatoci masu yawa daga baya, Flake ya yanke hukuncinsa.
Zabin Flake yana da ƙarfi, saboda a bayyane yake ‘yan jam’iyyar Republican ba za su sami kuri’u don yarda da Kavanaugh ba tare da bincike ba.
Shugaba Trump ya buɗe wani binciken FBI game da ƙage a kan Kavanaugh ɗin.
Firaministan Birtaniyya May ta kushe masu suka a kan Brexit da ‘yin siyasa’
Firaminista Theresa May ta soki masu suka na shirye-shiryenta na barin Tarayyar Turai da “maida abin siyasa” da makomar Birtaniyya da kuma zagon ƙasa ga abin da ƙasa ke sha’awa a cikin wata tattaunawa tare da jaridar Sunday Times.
Firaministan Birtaniyya Theresa May ta zo Taron Jam’iyyar Conservative a cikin Birmingham, Birtaniyya, a ranar 29 ga Satumba, 2018.
A cikin wata tattaunawar a gaba da wadda aka yi da ita a kan shafin gaba na jaridar, tsohon ministanta kan harkokin ƙasashen waje Boris Johnson ya tirjewa a kan harinsa na shirin Chequers ɗin nata don Brexit, yana cewa wani ƙudurin da ke cewa ya kamata Birtaniyya da Tarayyar Turai su karɓi kuɗaɗen fito na juna ya kasance “gaba ɗaya shirme ne.”
Harbin Wayde Sims ‘Yan sanda sun kama Dyteon Simpson da ake tuhuma a kan kisan ɗan wasan LSU.
‘Yan sanda sun kama wani da ake tuhuma a cikin mummunan harbi da ya kashe Wayde Sims, wani mai shekaru 20 kuma dan wasan ƙwallon kwando a LSU.
An kama Dyteon Simpson, mai shekaru 20 kuma an kai shi kurkuku a kan wata tuhumar kisa mai mataki na biyu, inji Ma’aikatar ‘Yan Sandan Baton Rouge.
Jami’ai sun saki bidiyo na takardamar tsakanin Sims da Simpson, kuma ‘yan sanda sun ce Sims ya rasa gilashinsa a lokacin fadan.
‘Yan sanda sun sami gilashin daga wurin da aka aikata laifin inda suka kuma ce sun sami abin halittar DNA na Simpson a kansu, kamar yadda rahoton WAFB mai alaƙa da CBS ya faɗa.
Bayan tambayan Simpson, ‘yan sanda sun ce ya amsa laifi na mummunan harbin Wayde.
An sa kuɗin belinsa a dala 350,000, a cewar rahoton Advocate.
Ofishin Mai Binciken a kan Musabbabin Kisa na Baton Rouge ta Gabas ya saki wani rahoton farko ranar Jumu’a, yana cewa musabbabin mutuwar wani harbin bindiga ne zuwa ga ka da ya wuce cikin wuya.
Ma’aikatar ta yabi jami’an ‘yan sanda na Jihar Louisiana masu aikin kama wanda ya gudu, da ɗakin ‘yan sanda na gwajin kimiyyar aikata lafi na jihar, da ‘yan sandan Jami’ar Kudanci da mazauna yanki don taimakawa a binciken da ya kai ga kamen.
Daraktan wasan tsalle-tsalle na LSU Joe Alleva ya gode wa ma’aikatan doka na yankin don irin aikinsu na “jajircewa da ganin an yi adalci.”
Shekarun Sims 20 ne.
Mai tsawon tattaki 6 da 6 ya girma ne a cikin Baton Rouge, inda mahaifinsa, Wayne, shi ma ya buga wasan ƙwallon kwando ga LSU.
Yana da matsakaicin maki 5.6 da sake dawo da ƙididdigar ci na 2.6 a wani na lokacin da shuɗe.
A ranar Juma’a da safe, mai horar da ‘yan wasan ƙwallon kwandon na LSU Will Wade ya ce ƙungiyar ta sami “tashin hankali” da “girgiza” da mutuwar ta Wayde.
“Wannan shi ne abin mutum yake damuwa game da shi a dukkan lokaci,” inji Wade.
Babban dutsi mai amon wuta ya fesa toka a kan Birnin Mexico
Toka da ke fesuwa daga babban dutsi mai amon wuta na Popocatepetl ta isa makwaɓta na kudancin babban birnin Mexico.
Cibiyar Hana Haɗura ta Ƙasa ta gargaɗi ‘yan Mexico a ranar Asabar kar su kusanci dutsin bayan abin ya kai koli a farfashewar inda kuma a ka yi rijistar fitar da hayaƙi na iskar gas 183 da kuma toka ta fiye da sa’o’i 24.
Cibiyar tana kula da cidodi da girgize-girgizen ƙasa.
Hotuna a hanyar sadarwa ta zumunta sun nuna mashimfiɗu marassa kauri na toka suna danƙare a jikin gilasan mota a cikin makwaɓta na Birnin Mexico kamar su Xochimilco.
Masana kimiyyar yanayi sun lura da wani karin aiki a dutsin da ke zaune a mil 45 (kilomita 72) kudu-maso-gabas na babban birnin tun daga wata girgizar kasa da aka yi mai girman 7.1 da ta raguza tsakiyar Mexico a Satumba 2017.
Dutsi mai amon wutar da ake kira "Don Goyo" ya daɗe yana tashi tun 1994.
’Yan sanda sun yi arangama da masu neman ɓallewa na Catalan kafin zagayowar bikin neman ‘yanci
An kama mutane shida a Barcelona a ranar Asabar bayan masu zanga-zangar nuna goyon bayan ‘yanci sun yi fito-na-fito tare da ‘yan sandan kwantar da tarzoma, kuma kamar yadda dubun-dubata suka shiga zanga-zanga ta adawa da juna don bikin zagayowar ranar kaɗa kuri’a da ta raba Catalonia a kan ɓallewa.
Wani gungu masu goyon bayan ɓallewar da suka rufe idanuwansu da ‘yan sanda suka riƙe sun jefe su da koyaye da kuma watsa musu fentin foda, inda suka ƙirƙiri wasu gajimare mai duhu a cikin titunan da yawanci sukan cika maƙil da ‘yan yawon shaƙatawa.
Faɗace-faɗace sun ɓarke a ranar daga baya inda ‘yan sanda suka yi amfani da kulaƙensu don hana faɗan.
Har fiye da tsawon sa’o’i masu yawa gungu-gungun masu goyon bayan ɓallewar suna amshi “Babu mantuwa, babu yafiya” sun yi rikici da masu zanga-zanga ‘yan son haɗewa suna ihu, Allah ya ja kwanan Spain.”
An yi magani a mutane goma sha huɗu don ƙananan raunuka da suka ji a zanga-zangogi, kamar yadda kafofin watsa labarai na gida suka ba da rahoto.
Har yanzu da tashin hankali sosai a lardin da ya sa ‘yanci a zuciyarsa shekara ɗaya bayan zaɓen raba gardama na 1 ga Oktoba wanda Madrid ke ɗauka ba ya bisa doka amma ‘yan Catalan masu neman ɓallewa ke ta yin murna da shi.
Masu jefa kuri’ar sun yi zaɓe sosai inda suka zaɓi ‘yanci kodayake ba a fito sosai ba inda waɗanda ba sa son ɓallewa suka ƙauracewa zaɓen.
A cewar hukumomin Catalan an aƙalla raunata mutane 1000 ne shekarar da ta wuce bayan ‘yan sanda sun yi ƙoƙarin su tsaida kaɗa kuri’ar da ake yi a wuraren jefa kuri’ar a dukkan faɗin lardin a cikin gumurzun tashin hankali.
Gungu-gungu na masu nuna goyon bayan ‘yanci sun yi dandazo waje da dare suna goyon baya na ‘yan sandan ƙasa.
Zanga-zangar ta ci gaba amma an tilasta mata ɗaukan wata hanya daban.
Narcis Termes, mai shekaru 68, wani latirisha da ke halartar zanga-zangar ‘yan neman ɓallewar tare da matarsa ya ce ba ya kuma fatan ganin yiwuwar Catalonia ta sami ‘yanci.
“Shekarar da ta wuce mun rayu a cikin ɗaya daga cikin lokacinmu mafi kyau.
Na kalli iyayena suna kukan murna saboda damar jefa kuri’a amma yanzu mun tsaya ciki,” inji shi.
Duk da gudanar da wata muhimmiyar nasara ko da tsukekkiya ce a cikin zaɓuɓɓukan yankin a Disamba da ta wuce, jam’iyyun da ke goyon bayan ‘yanci na Catalan sun yi gwagwarmaya don su ci gaba da hazaƙar wannan shekarar tare da yawancin sanannun fitattun shugabanninsu ko dai sun tafi neman mafakar da suka sa kansu ko an kame su suna jiran shari’a don rawarsu da suka taka a cikin shirya zaɓen raba gardamar da furuci na ‘yanci da suka yi daga baya.
Joan Puig, wani makanike mai shekaru 42 da ke daukan zanga-zanga a cikin goyon baya na ‘yan sanda a kan tarho dinsa, ya ce rikicin ya sami ruruwa ne daga ‘yan siyasa da ke dukkan bangarorin.
“Yana ƙara ƙazanta sosai,” inji shi.
A ranar Asabar, Oriol Junqueras, ɗaya daga shugabanni tara na Catalan da ke tsare kafin a fara shari’a tun ƙarshen shekarar da ta wuce, ya sanar cewa zai tsaya zaɓuɓɓukan Majalisar Dokoki ta Turai a shekara mai zuwa.
“Tsayawa a matsayin wani ɗan takara don zaɓuɓɓukan Turai shi ne hanya mafi kyau ta kin koma baya a kimomin dimokuraɗiyya da zalunci da muka gani daga gwamnatin Spain,” inji shi.
Londonderry: An kama masu maza bayan an doka mota a gida
An kama wasu maza, masu shekaru 33, 34 da 29, bayan an ta maimaita doka wata ƙaramar mota zuwa cikin wani gida a da ke Londonderry.
Abin ya faru ne a cikin Ballynagard Crescent a ranar Alhamis da kusan ƙarfe 19:30 BST.
Mataimakin Sufeto Bob Blemmings ya ce an lalata ƙofofi da ma gidan kansa.
An kuma harba ƙila kwari da baka a kan ƙaramar motar a wani lokaci.
Cin da Menga ya yi ba wa Livingston nasara 1 da 0 a kan Rangers
Cin ƙwallon Dolly Menga ya ba wa Livingston samun nasara
Livingston da aka ƙara wa girma ta ba da mamaki ga Rangers inda ta ajiye Steven Gerrard kawai zuwa ga cinsa da aka yi karo na biyu a cikin wasanni 18 a matsayinsa na manaja na kulob ɗin Ibrox.
Harin da Dolly Menga ya yi ya kasance abin da kawo bambanci saboda ɓangaren Gary Holt ya motsa lebur tare da Hibernian a cikin mataki na biyu.
Ɓangaren Gerrard yana nan ba tare da wata nasara da zai ta fi da ita ba a cikin wasan Premiership ɗin wannan lokacin kuma zai fuskanci Leaders Hearts, waɗanda suke bi da digo takwas, Lahadi mai zuwa.
Kafin nan, Rangers sun karɓi Rapid Vienna a cikin wasan Europa League a ranar Alhamis.
A lokacin da ake ciki hakan, Livinsgton, sun kara matsayinsu na ba wanda ya doke su a cikin shiyyar zuwa wasanni shida, tare da shugaban horar da wasa Holt har yanzu don ɗanɗana dokewa tun da ya maye gurbin Kenny Miler wata da ya wuce.
Livingston sun rasa damammaki a kan maziyartansu da ba su dama
Ya kamata a ce ƙungiyar Holt suna gaba ne kafin su ci, tare da fuskantar tasu wanda ke haifar wa Rangers matsaloli iri-iri.
Scott Robinson ya shige ciki amma ya ja ƙoƙarinsa ta gaban fuska ta cin nasara, shi ke nan Alan Lithgow kawai zai iya fuskantar da ƙoƙarinsa bayan yin ƙasa don haɗuwa da bugu da ka na cin Craig Halkett.
Masu saukan bakin sun yarda su bar Rangers su buga wasa a gabansu, suna sane da cewa za su iya wahalar da masu ziyarar a jerin ɗaiɗaiku.
Kuma wancan shi ne yadda ci mai muhimmancin ya gudana.
Rangers sun amince da bugun da ba tarewa kuma Livingston suka yi aiki da wata dama, Declan Gallagher da Robinson suka haɗe suka tsara Menga, wanda ya taɓa da kuma ci daga tsakiya ta akwatin.
A wannan mataki, Rangers ta mamaye riƙe ƙwallo amma ta sami tsaron gidan ba zai ba da damar wucewa ba kuma mai kama ƙwallo Liam Kelly kuma gaba ɗaya bai damu ba.
Wannan yanayi ya ci gaba har rabi na biyu, kodayake Alfredo Morelos ya tilasta wani ceto daga Kelly.
Scott Pittman bai samu dama ba daga ƙafa ta mai kama ƙwallo na Rangers Allan McGregor kuma Lithgow ya buɗa sosai daga wani wasan da Livingston ya tsara.
Sai kuma bugu ta ko’ina da suka riƙa zuwa cikin akwatin Livingston inda kuma a ci gaba da maganinsu, a yayin da aka samu bugu daga kai sai gola - bayan ƙalubalantar Halkett a kan maye gurbin Glenn Middleton, kuma ɗaya don taɓawa da hannu - inda aka ture gefe.
‘Abin mamaki’ daga Livingston - nazari
Alasdair Lamont Scotland a Yanki na Tony Macaroni
Wani wasa mai ban mamaki da sakamako don Livingston.
Ga wani mutum, sun burge sosai, suna ci gaba da wuce abin da ake tsammani a kan wannan abin da ya yi saman.
Irin salonsu na wasa da ma’aikata ya dan canza tun da dawowarsu zuwa saman matsayi, amma babban yabo ya kamata ya je ne ga Holt da irin hanyar da ya haɗa ƙungiyar tun zuwansa.
Yana da gwarzaye da yawa.
Kyaftin Halkett ya shirya, inda ya yi ta tsara wani tsaro mai kyau, a lokacin da Menga ya sa Connor Goldson da Joe Worrall suka kasance a kan ƙafafunsu gaba ɗaya.
Rangers sun kusan rasa ƙarfin gwiwa, kusan.
Duk da irin yadda suke da kyau a lokutan a ƙarƙashin Gerrard, sun gaza samun irin wadannan daidaituwar.
Ƙwallonsu ta ƙarshe ba ta isa ba - kawai sau ɗaya ne suka yanke gefen gidan a buɗe - kuma wani abu ne na wartsakarwar kira ga Rangers, waɗanda suka sami kansu a cikin tsakiyar teburi.
Erdogan ya sami wata irin karɓa a Cologne
An ga murmurshi iri-iri da shuɗin sararin samaniya a ranar Asabar (29 ga Satumba) inda shugabannin Turkiyya da Jamus suka haɗu don cin kumallon safe a cikin Berlin.
A cikin ranarta ta ƙarshen ziyarar Shugaba Erdogan mai rikitarwa zuwa Jamus - wanda aka tsara don gyara hulɗoɗi tsakanin ƙawayen NATO din.
Sun sami rashin jituwa a kan wasu batutuwa da suka haɗa da ‘yancin ɗan Adam, ‘yancin ‘yan jarida da shigar Turkiyyar zuwa Tarayyar Turai.
Erdogan daga nan ya wuce Cologne don buɗe wani ƙaton sabon masallaci.
Birnin gida ne ga mutanen Turkiyya da suka fi yawa a wajen Turkiyyar.
‘Yan sanda sun kawo maganar dalilan tsaro don toshe wani dandazon jama’a na kusan 25,000 daga taro da ke gaban masallacin, amma masu goyon baya da yawa sun bayyana a kusa don ganin shugaban nasu.
Ɗaruruwan masu zanga-zanga da ke adawa da Erdogan - mafi yawansu Kurɗawa - sun bayyana muryoyinsu, suna Allah-wa-dai gaba ɗaya da ƙudurorin Erdogan da hukuncin da gwamnatin Jamus ta yanke ɗin na maraba da shi zuwa ƙasar.
Zanga-zangogin na wurin suna nuna fasalin rabuwa na zuwan wani maziyarci da Turkawan Jamus ke yaba a matsayin wani gwarzo da kuma tsana a matsayin mai-kama-karya ga sauran.
Haɗarin hanya na Deptford : Matukin keke ya mutu a sanadin karo da mota
Wani matuƙin keke ya mutu a cikin wani karo da ya haɗa da wata ƙaramar mota a cikin Landan.
Karon ya faru ne kusa da mahaɗar Titin Bestwood da Titin  Evelyn, wata hanya mai cunkoso a cikin Deptford, a cikin kudu-maso-gabas na birnin, da kusan ƙarfe 10:15 BST.
Direban motar ya tsaya kuma ma’aikatan kawo ɗaukin jinya sun zo, amma mutumin ya mutu a wurin da abin ya faru.
Karon ya faru ne watanni bayan wani matuƙin keken ya mutu a cikin wani haɗarin kaɗi-a-gudu a kan Titin Childers, kusan wani mil guda daga wurin karon na ranar Asabar.
‘Yan sandan Birni sun ce jami’ai suna aiki don gane mutumin da sanar da danginsa.
An rufe hanyoyi da sauya hanyar bas kuma an ba da shawara ga matukan motoci su guje wa yankin.
Kurkukun Long Lartin:  Jami’ai shida sun ji rauni a rikici
An ji rauni a jami’ai shida a cikin tashin hankali a wani kurkukun maza mai tsaro sosai, inji Ofishin Kurkukun.
Tashin hankalin ya ɓarke ne a HMP Long Lartin a cikin Worcestershire da kusan ƙarfe 09:30 BST a ranar Lahadi kuma yana ci gaba.
An kawo ƙwararrun jami’an "Tornado" don su magance tashin hankalin, wanda ya ƙunshi fursunoni takwas kuma an taƙaita shi zuwa ga ɓangare ɗaya.
An yi magani ga jami’an don raunukan fuska a wurin da abin ya faru.
A cewar mai magana da yawun Ma’aikatar Kurkuku: “An tura ƙwararrun ma’aikatan da aka horar don magance wani abin da ke faruwa a HMP Long Lartin.
An yi magani a mambobi na ma’aikatan shida don raunuka da suka samu.
Ba ma zuba ido ga tashin hankali a cikin kurkukunmu, kuma sun bayyana cewa za a tura waɗanda ke da hannu kuma akwai yiwuwar su jima a bayan kantoci.”
HMP Long Lartin ɗin yana riƙe da fiye da fursunoni 500, da suka haɗa da wasu daga cikin masu laifi mafiya haɗari na ƙasar.
A cikin watan Yuni an kawo rahoto cewa gwamnan kurkukun ya karɓi kulawar asibiti bayan wani fursuna ya kai masa hari.
Kuma a cikin watan Oktoba na shekarar da ta wuce jami’an kwantar da tarzoma sun magance wani mummunan tashin hankali inda aka farma hari a kan ma’aikata da ƙwallayen wasa.
Babbar Guguwar Rosa Tana Barazana a Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake City Da Ambaliyar Ruwa Mai Tasowa (Yankuna Masu Fari Za Su Ƙila More)
Bai cika faruwa a ce wani raguwar zafi ya tasamma Arizona ba, amma wannan shi ne abin da ƙila ya faru da wuri mako mai zuwa kamar yadda sauran ƙarfin Guguwar Rosan ke bin diddigi a faɗin Hamadar Kudu-maso-gabas, inda take samar da haɗuran ambaliyar ruwa mai tasowa.
Ma’aikatar Hasashen Yanayi ta Ƙasa ta riga ta fitar da bayanan kallo game da ambaliyar mai tasowa ta Litinin da Talata don Arizona a cikin kudanci da gabashin Nevada, kudu-maso-gabas na California da Utah, da ya haɗa da birane na  Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas, da Salt Lake City.
Ana tsammanin Rosa ɗin za ta ɗauki wata hanya ta saman Phoenix a ranar Talata, tana turawa zuwa ƙarshen Litinin tare da ruwan sama.
Ma’aikatar Hasashen Yanayi ta Ƙasa da ke cikin Phoenix ta lura a cikin wani bayani da ta fitar ta Twitter cewa kawai “Munanan haɗarin iska guda goma sun samar da cidar lokacin zafi ko matsayin raguwa tsakanin mil 200 na Phoenix  tun daga shekarun 1950!
Katrina (1967) da wata guguwa ce tsakanin mil 40 na iyakar Arizona.”
Samfurorin Cibiyar Guguwar Iska ta Ƙasa mafi sabunta sun yi kintacen incina 2 zuwa 4 na ruwan sama, tare da ‘yan incina har kusan 6 da ba sa ciki a cikin Mogollon Rim na Arizona.
Sauran yankunan na Desert Southwest da suka hada da tsakiyar Rockies da Great Basin ba mamaki su sami incina 1 zuwa 2 tare da jimillar da ba ta ciki har kusan incina 4 da zai yiwu.
Ga waɗanda ba sa cikin haɗarin ambaliyar mai tasowar, ruwan saman na Rosa ɗin ƙila ya zama wata rahama tun da yankin yana fama da fari.
Kodayake ambaliyar ruwa wani abin damuwa ne sosai, wani daga cikin wannan ruwan saman zai fa’idantar tun da Kudu-maso-yamma a yanzu yana ganin yanayi na fari.
A cewar Hukumar Kula da Fari ta Amurka, kawai sama da kashi 40 cikin ɗari ne na Arizona ke ganin aƙalla matsanancin fari, nau’i mafi girma na biyu,” inji rahoto na weather.com.
Da farko, hanyar Guguwar Rosa ta wuce ne zuwa faɗuwa a ƙasa ta cikin zirin Baja California na Mexico.
Rosa, har yanzu tana da ƙarfin ba babbar iskar guguwa da safiyar Lahadi tare da gayar iskoki na mil 85 a kowace sa’a, shi ne mil 385 kudu da Punta Eugenia, Mexico kuma tana matsawa a mil 12 kowace sa’a.
Cidar tana haɗuwa da ruwa mai sanyi a cikin tekun Pacific don haka tana sauka.
A saboda haka, ana tsammani za ta sauka a ƙasa a cikin Mexico a ƙarfin cidar lokacin zafi da cikin rana ko yamma a ranar Litinin.
Ba mamaki ruwan sama a faɗin sassa na Mexico ya zama da yawa, yana mai haifar da wani haɗarin ambaliya mai yawa.
“Ana tsammanin jimillar ruwan sama na incina 3 zuwa 6 daga Baja California zuwa cikin kudu-maso-yammacin Sonora,” a cewar rahoton weather.com.
Daga nan Rosa za ta bi arewa ta faɗin Mexico a matsayin cidar iskar zafi kafin isa iyakar Arizona a cikin farkon sa’o’in safiyar Talata a matsayin raguwar lokacin zafi, inda daga nan za ta bi sama ta cikin Arizona da kuma zuwa cikin kudancin Itah da ƙarshen Talata da dare.
“Babban haɗari da ake tsammani daga Rosa ko abubuwanta da za su saura shi ne ruwan sama sosai a cikin Baja California, arewa-maso-yammacin Sonora, da Amurka Desert Southwest," inji Cibiyar Iskar Guguwa ta Ƙasa.
Ana tsammanin wannan ruwayen su samar da ambaliyar ruwan sama mai tasowa da zubar burbushi a cikin hamada, da yankewar ƙasa a cikin yankunan tsaunuka.
Harin Midsomer Norton:  Kame mutane huɗu da suka yi ƙoƙarin kisa
An kame wasu yara su uku da wani mutum mai shekaru 20 a kan zargin ƙoƙarin yin kisa bayan an sami wani mai shekaru 16 da raunukan caka wuka a cikin Somerset.
An sami yaron ne da raunin a cikin yankin Farfajiyar Excelsior na Midsomer Norton, da kusan ƙarfe 04:00 BST na ranar Asabar.
An ɗauke zuwa asibiti inda yake cikin wani yanayi “mai ƙarko.”
An kama wani mai shekaru 17, biyu masu shekaru 18 da wani mutum mai shekaru 20 da dare a cikin yankin Radstock, Avon inji ‘Yan Sandan Somerset.
Jami’ai sun roƙi duk wani wanda ƙila ke da ƙaramin bidiyo na wayar hannu na abin da ya faru da ya zo.
Trump ya ce Kavanaugh ‘ya sha wahala, bakin hali, fushi’ na Jam’iyyar Democrat
“Wata kuri’a don Alkali Kavanaugh kaɗa kuri’a ne don ƙin rashin tausayi da dabarun fin ƙarfi na Jam’iyyar Democrat,” inji Trump a wani gangami a cikin Wheeling, West Virginia.
Trump ya ce Kavanaugh ya sha “wahalar rashin tausayi, fushi” na Jam’iyyar Democrat ta hanyar tura sunansa.
Kavanaugh ya ba da shaida a gaban Congress a ranar Alhamis, da ƙarfi yana kuma cikin fushi na ƙin wani ƙage daga Christine Blasey Ford cewa ya far mata ta hanyar jima’i shekaru da yawa da suka wuce suna samari.
Ford ita ma ta ba shaida a jin bahasin game da ƙagen nata.
Shugaban ya faɗa a rana Asabar cewa “Amurkawa sun ga fasaha da kyau da ƙarfin hali” na Kavanaugh wannan ranar.
“Wata kaɗa kuri’a don tabbatar da Alkali Kavanaugh West jefa kuri’a ne don tabbatar da ɗaya daga cikin masana shari’a da suka cimma rayuwa a wannan lokacin namu, wani masanin shari’a da ke da fitaccen rubutaccen labari na aikin jama’a,” ya faɗa a dandazon jama’a magoya baya na Virginia ta Yamma.
Shugaban ya ɗan yi tsokaci ne game da tura sunan Kavanaugh a yayin da yake magana game da amfani na fitowar ‘yan Republican a cikin zaɓuɓɓukan tsakiyar zango.
“Saura makonni biyar zuwa ɗaya daga cikin zaɓuɓɓuka mafi muhimmanci a lokutan rayuwarmu.
Ba zan tsaya ba, amma a zahiri zan tsaya,” inji shi.
“Shi ne ya sa nake ko’ina ina yaƙi don manyan ‘yan takara.”
Trump cikin mahawara ‘yan Democrat suna kan wata manufa ne ta “ƙi da taka burki.”
Ana tsammanin farkon babban hanyar bi don kaɗa kuri’a a  daɗen Majalisar Dattawa a kan zaɓen Kavanaugh da za a yi da ba zai wuce Juma’a ba, a faɗar wani mai taimaka wa babban shugaba na GOP kamar yadda ya ce wa CNN.
Ɗaruruwa sun mace a sakamakon girgizar ƙasar Indonesiya, kuma ganin ƙarin mutuwar
Aƙalla an kashe mutane 384, da tafiya da wasu saboda igiyoyin ruwa masu girma sun fado a kan bakin teku, a lokacin da wata babbar girgizar ƙasa da tsunami suka afka a tsibirin Sulawesi na Indonesiya, injin hukumomi a ranar Asabar.
Ɗaruruwan mutane suka taru don wani biki a kan teku na birnin Palu a ranar Juma’a a yayin da igiyoyin ruwan da suka mitoci shiɗa a sama (taku 18) suka afka bakin teku da dare, inda suka share da yawa suka mutu da lalata kowane abu da ke hanyar tasu.
Tsunamin ta biyo bayan wata girgizar ƙasa mai ƙarfin 7 da ɗigo 5.
“A yayin da barazanar tsunamin ta taso jiya, mutane a lokacin suna ayyukansu ne a kan bakin tekun kuma ba su gudu nan da nan ba inda suka zama waɗanda abin ya shafa,” inji Sutopo Purwo Nugroho, mai magana da yawun hukumar rage haɗura ta Indonesiya ta BNPB a cikin wata gajeruwar ganawa da ‘yan jarida a cikin Jakarta.
“Tsunamin tazo da kanta ne, ta jawo ƙananan motoci, katakwaye, gidaje, ta kuma bugi duk abin da ke kan ƙasa,” inji Nugroho, inda ya kara da cewa tsunami ta yi tafiya a faɗin buɗeɗɗen teku da gudu na kilomita 800 kowace sa’a (mil 497 kowace sa’a) kafin ta sauka a bakin tekun.
Wasu mutanen sun hau bishiyoyi ne don tsira daga tsunami kuma sun rayu, inji shi.
An kwashe kusan mutane 16,700 zuwa cibiyoyi 24 da ke cikin Palu.
Hotunan da aka ɗauka daga sama da hukumar haɗarin ta sake sun nuna gine-gine da shaguna a lalace, gadojin sun lankwashe da rushewa da wani masallaci ruwa ya kewaye shi.
An ci gaba da samun girgize-girgize na baya da suka addabi birnin da ke kusa da tekun a ranar Asabar.
An ji girgize-girgizen ƙasa a jere a wani yanki mai mutane miliyan 2 da dubu ɗari 4.
Hukumar Auna da Aiwatar da Fasaha ta Indonesiya (BPPT) a cikin wata sanarwa ta ce ƙarfi da babbar girgizar ƙasa ta sake a ranar Jumu’ar ya kai kusan sau 200 na ƙarfin bam na sinadarin atom da aka jefa a kan Hiroshima a cikin Yakin Duniya na Biyu.
Yanayi na birnin, wanda ke zaune a ƙarshe na wani ɗan ƙaramin ziri mai tsawo, ƙila shi ya faɗaɗa girma na tsunami ɗin, inji ta.
Nugroho ya bayyana lalacewar a matsayin “mai yawa” kuma ya ce dubun-dubata na gidaje, asibitoci, shagunan cinikayya da otel-otel duk sun ruguje.
An sami gawarwakin waɗanda abin ya shafa a maƙale a ƙarƙashin gine-gine da suka rushe, inji shi, ya kuma ƙara da cewa mutane 540 sun ji rauni kuma an rasa 29.
Nugroho ya ce yawan masu mutuwar da lalacewar zai ƙaru sosai a layin bakin teku kilomita 300 (mil 190) arewa da Palu, wani yanki da ake kira Donggala,
Sadarwa “gaba ɗaya sun tsaya cik kuma babu labari” daga Donggala, jinji Nugroho.
Akwai fiye da mutane 300,000 da ke zauna a can,” inji ƙungiyar agaji ta Red Cross a cikin wata sanarwa, tana mai ƙarin cewa ma’aikatanta da masu sa-kai sun nufi yankunan da abin ya shafa.
“Wannan tuni wani bala’i ne, amma zai iya ƙara muni,” inji ta.
An soki hukumar a ranar Asabar sosai don rashin sanarwa cewa wata tsunami za ta afka wa Palu, kodayake jami’ai sun ce igiyoyin ruwa sun zo a tsakanin lokacin da aka fitar da gargaɗin.
Wani bidiyon da ba ƙwararre ba da aka raba ta kafar sada zumunta za a iya jin wani mutum a kan saman daɓe na wani gini yana ihun girgiza gargaɗi na kusantowar tsunami ga mutane da ke titin ƙasan.
A cikin mintina wani bango na ruwa ya faɗo a kan tekun, yana ɗaukewa gine-gine da ƙananan motoci.
Kamfanin dillacin labarai na Reuters ba iya tantance bidiyon ba nan da nan.
Girgizar ƙasar da tsunamin sun haifar da katsewar lantarki da yanke sadarwa a kewayen Palu inda ya haifar da wahala ga hukumomi wajen haɗin gamayyar ƙoƙare-ƙoƙare na ceto.
Sojoji sun fara aika manyan jiragen ɗaukan kaya da tallafi daga Jakarta da sauran birane, inji hukumomi, amma waɗanda aka kwashen har yanzu suna sosai buƙatar abinci da sauran muhimman kayayyaki.
An sake buɗe filin jirgin sama na birnin kaɗai don ƙoƙare-ƙoƙaren kayan agaji kuma zai kasance a rufe sai har Octoba.
An tsara Shugaba Joko Widodo zai ziyarci cibiyoyin kwashewa mutane a cikin Palu a ranar Lahadi.
Ƙididdigar Mutuwar Tsunami a Indonesiya Ta Haura 800
Abin Ya Ɓaci Sosai.
Kodayake ma’aikatan World Vision sun koma birnin Palu lafiya ƙalau daga Donggala, inda ma’aikatan ke zaune a matsugunan tanfol da aka kafa a farfajiyar ofishin nasu, sun nuna wani hali na rugujewa a kan hanyar, inji Mista Doseba.
“Sun faɗa mun sun ga gidaje da yawa da suka rushe,” inji shi.
Abin ya ɓaci sosai.
Duk da gungu-gungun ‘yan agaji da suka fara wata babbar hoɓɓasa ta fara aikin tallafi na bala’i, wasu sun yi ƙorafi cewa ma’aikatan agaji na waje da ke ƙwarewa sosai ana hana su tafiya zuwa Palu.
A cewar ƙa’idojin Indonesiya, kashe kuɗaɗe, samarwa da ba da ma’aikata daga ƙasashen waje kawai zai fara ne idan an furta wuri na fitina a matsayin zango na bala’i na ƙasa.
Hakan har yanzu bai faru ba.
“Har yanzu wani lebur ne yankin bala’i,” inji Aulia Arriani, mai magana da yawun Red Cross ta Indonesiya.
Da zarar gwamnatin ta ce, “Ya yi, wannan zai zama wani bala’i na ƙasa,” za mu buɗe don taimakon ƙasa-da-ƙasa amma babu matsayin har yanzu.”
Kamar yadda dare na biyu ya faɗa kan Palu bayan girgizar ƙasa da tsunami ta ranar Jumu’a, abokai da iyali na waɗanda suka ɓata suna ta fatan cewa ‘yan uwan nasu za su zama mu’ujizozi da za su rayar da layukan labari marar daɗi na bala’o’i na ƙasa.
A ranar Asabar, an ciro wani ƙaramin yaro daga wata matattar datti.
A ranar Lahadi, masu ceto sun ‘yantar da wata mata wanda ta kasance tana ƙarƙashin burbushi na kwanaki biyu tare da gawar mahaifiyarta kusa da ita.
Gendon Subandono, mai horar da ‘yan wasa na Ɗƙungiyar ‘yan sauka daga sama na Indonesiya, ya horar da ‘yan wasan biyu da suka bace na Wasannin Asiya, wanda aka gama a farkon wannan watan a cikin Indonesiya.
Saura daga cikin waɗanda aka rutsa da su a otel ɗin Roa Roa, har da Mista Mandagi, ɗalibansa ne.
“A matsayi wani babba a cikin wasan saukowa daga saman, ni ma ina nawa taƙaicin da nake ji,” inji shi.
Mista Gendon ya ba da bayanin yadda aka yi, a cikin sa’o’i bayan labarin rushewar otel ɗin Roa Roa da aka watsa a tsakanin al’ummar wasan saukowa daga saman, ya aika sakonnin WhatsApp a dugunzume zuwa masu gasa ta Palu, waɗanda ke shiga cikin bikin na bakin tekun.
Sakonninsa, kodayake, kawai sun haifar da alamar launin toka guda mai zane, a maimakon wani guda biyu na zane-zane shudi.
“Ina jin yana nufi ba a aika sakonni ne ba,” inji shi.
Ɓarayi sun ɗauki dala 26,750 a lokacin sake cika ATM a Newport a kan Daɓe
Ɓarayi a ranar Juma’a da safe sun sace dala 26,750 daga wurin wani ma’aikacin Brink da ke sake cika wani ATM a Newport a kan Daɓe, a cewar wani labari da aka sake daga Ma’aikatar ‘Yan Sanda ta Newport.
Direban ƙaramar motar yana cirewa wani ATM a cikin wani gini na nishaɗi da shiryawa don kawo ƙarin kuɗi, Det. Dennis McCarthy ya rubuta a cikin sanarwar.
A lokacin da yake cikin aiki, wani mutum “ya zo a guje daga bayan ma’aikacin na Brink” kuma ya saci jakar kuɗi da za a kawo.
Shaidun gani da ido sun ga waɗanda ake zargi da yawa suna gudu daga wurin da aka yi laifin a cewar sanarwar, amma ‘yan sanda ba su fayyace yawan waɗanda ke cikin ba.
Ya kamata duk wani da ke da bayani game da shaidarsu ya tuntuɓi ‘yan sandan Newport a kan 859-292-3680.
Kanye West: Mawaƙin Rap ya canza sunansa zuwa Ye
Mawaƙin Rap yana canza sunan - zuwa Ye.
A sanar da canza sunan ta Twitter a ranar Asabar, ya rubuta: “A da an san ni a matsayin Kanye West.”
Ana yi wa lakabi da Ye ga West, mai shekaru 41 na tsawon wani lokaci kuma ya yi amfani da moniker a sunan faifansa na takwas, wanda aka sake a cikin Yuni.
Canjin yana zuwa ne kafin bayyanarsa a cikin shirin Saturday Night Live, inda ake tsammanin zai ƙaddamar da sabon faifansa Yandhi.
Yana maye gurbin mawaƙi Ariana Grande a shirin wanda ya soke don “dalilin ɓacin rai,” inji maƙirƙirin shirin.
Kamar yadda ya zama abu gajartacce na sunansa na sana’a na yanzu, West a da ya ce kalmar tana da wata ma’anar addini a gare shi.
“Na yi imani ‘ye’ kalma ce da aka fi amfani sosai a cikin Baibul, kuma a cikin Baibul tana nufin ‘kai,” inji West a farkon wannan shekarar, yana tattauna sunan faifan ɗinsa tare da mai karɓan baƙi na rediyo Big Boy.
“Don haka ni ku ne, mu ne.
Ya wuce ne daga Kanye, wanda ke nufin guda ɗaya, zuwa kaɗai Ye - kawai wani manuni na kyawunmu, ruɗaninmu, kowane abu.
Faifan kamar wani nuni ne na su wane ne mu.”
Yana daga cikin sanannun rappers da suka canza sunansu.
An san Sean Combs da sunaye iri-iri a matsayin Puff Daddy, P. Diddy ko Diddy, amma wannan shekarar ya sanar cewa fifikonsa na sunayen Love da Brother Love ne.
Wani abokin haɗin gwiwa na West, JAY-Z, shi ma ya sha yi da ko ba tare da wani layi gajere na tsakiyar kalma da manyan baƙaƙe.
AMLO na Mexico ya yi alkawarin ba zai yi amfani da sojoji a kan fararen hula ba
Zaɓaɓɓen Shugaban Ƙasar Mexico Andres Manuel Lopez Obrador ya yi alkawarin ba zai taɓa yin amfani da ƙarfin soja a kan fararen hula ba a yayin da ƙasar ke kusantar cika shekaru 50 na wani murƙushewar da aka yi wa ɗalibai da aka zubar da jini.
Lopez Obrador ya yi alkawari ranar Asabar a Tlatelolco Plaza “kar a taɓa ko kaɗan amfani da sojoji wajen murƙushe mutanen Mexico.”
Rundunonin sun yi harbi a kan wata zanga-zangar lumana a cibiyar a ranar 2 ga Oktoba, 1968, inda suka kashe da yawa har mutane 300 a wani lokaci yayin da ɗalibai ‘yan gwagwarmayar ra’ayin gurguzu suka fara samun matsuguni a Latin America.
Lopez Obrador ya yi alkawari na goyon bayan samari ‘yan Mexico ta ba da tallafe-tallafe na wata-wata ga waɗanda ke karatu kuma da buɗe ƙarin jami’o’i na gwamnati kyauta.
Ya kuma ce rashin aikin yi da wani rashi na damammakin ilmi su ne ke jan samari zuwa gungun ƙungiyoyi masu aikata laifi.
Ya kamata Amurka ta ruɓanya kuɗin A.I.
Kamar yadda China ta zama tana aiki sosai a cikin hikimar da ba ta asali ba, ya kamata Amurka ta ruɓanya yawan abin da take kashewa a cikin nazari da ke cikin filin, inji mai zuba jari mai gwada hikimar da ba ta asalin ba Kai-Fu Lee, wanda ya yi aiki da Google, Microsoft da Apple.
Sharhohin suna zuwa ne bayan ɓangarori da dama na gwamnatin Amurka sun yi furuci a kan AI na hikimar da ba ta asalin ba, duk da cewa Amurka ta rasa wata dabarar AI a  tsare.
A halin da ake cikin, China ta gabatar da shirinta shekarar da ta wuce: tana ƙoƙarin ta zama ta farko a cikin ƙago AI a shekara ta 2030.
“Ruɓanya kasafin kuɗi na AI zai zama wani mafari mai kyau, ganin cewa dukkan sauran ƙasashe sun yi gaba sosai a bayan Amurka kuma muna neman wani sabon abu a cikin AI,” inji Lee.
Ruɓanya kashe kuɗi zai iya rubanya damammaki inda za a cimma babban AI na gaba a cikin Amurka, Lee ya ce wa CNBC a cikin wata intabiyu wannan makon.
Lee, wanda Houghton Mifflin Harcourt ya buga littafinsa "AI Superpowers: China, Silicon Valley and the New World Order"  wannan watan, shi ne Babban Shugaba na Sinovation Ventures China, wanda ya zuba jari a cikin daya daga sanannun kamfanonin AI a cikin China, Face++.
A cikin shekaru na 1980 a Jami’ar Carnegie Mellon ya yi aiki a kan wani tsarin AI da ya doke ɗan wasan Amurka Othello da ya fi matsayi, daga baya kuma ya zama wani zababben shugaba a Microsoft Research da shugaban Google na reshen China.
Lee ya faɗi gasa ta baya ta gwamnatin Amurka a kan fasaha kamar Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge inda ya tambaya yaushe ne za a yi na gaban, saboda ya taimaka gane masu hange nesa na gaba.
Manazarta a cikin Amurka yawanci sukan yi aiki tuƙuru saboda cin taimakon kuɗaɗen gwamnati, inji Lee.
“Ba China ne ke ɗaukewa shugabannin ilmi ba; kamfanoni ne,” inji Lee.
Facebook, Google da sauran kamfanonin fasaha sun ɗauki hayar manyan masu ilmi daga jami’o’i don aiki a kan AI a shekarun kwana nan.
Lee ya ce canje-canjen ƙudurin shiga ƙasa zai iya kuma taimakon Amurka ta daga ƙoƙare-ƙoƙarenta na AI.
“Ina jin ya kamata korayen katina su zama kai-tsaye ake samar da su ga masu digirin-digirgir a fannin hikimar AI da ba ta asali ba,” inji shi.
Majalisar Ƙasar China ta fitar da Shirin Ci Gaban Hikimar Da Ba Ta Asali Don Al’ummar Gaba nata a cikin Yulin 2017.
Gidauniyar Kimiyya na Halitta ta Ƙasa ta China ta samar da kuɗaɗe ga mutane a makarantun ilmi irin zuwa ga hanyar da Gidauniyar Kimiyyar ta Ƙasa da sauran hukumomin gwamnati ke ba da kuɗi ga manazartan Amurka, amma yanayin darajar aikin ilmi ya yi ƙasa a cikin China, inji Lee.
A farkon wannan shekarar Ma’aikatar Tsaro ta Amurka ta kafa wata Cibiyar Hikimar Da Ba Ta Asali Ba, wanda aka shirya don ta sa abokan hulɗa daga masana’anta da makaranta, kuma fadar White House ta sanar da ƙirƙirar wani Zaɓaɓɓen Kwamiti a kan Hikimar da ba ta asali ba.
Kuma wannan watan DARPA ta sanar da zuba jarin dala biliyan 2 a cikin wani ƙoƙari da ake kira AI Next.
A game da NSF, a yanzu haka ta zuba jarin fiye da dala miliyan 100 a kowace shekara a cikin binciken AI.
A halin da ake ciki yanzu, dokar Amurka da ke neman ƙirƙirar wata Hukumar Tsaron Ƙasa kan Hikimar Da Ba Asali tana nan ba ta ga wani aiki ba a cikin watanni.
‘Yan Macedonia suna jefa kuri’ar raba gardama a kan ko a canza sunan ƙasar
Mutanen Macedonia sun jefa kuri’a a cikin wata raba gardama a ranar Lahadi ko ta canza sunanta zuwa “Jamhuriyyar Arewacin Macedonia,” a wani yinƙuri da zai warware wata tsohuwar taƙaddama tare da Greece wadda ta toshe nemanta na zama mamba don Tarayyar Turai da NATO.
Greece, wadda ke da wani yanki da ake kira Macedonia, ya nace da cewa sunan makwabciyarta ta arewa yana wakiltar wani nema ne a kan iyakarta kuma ta hau-kujerar-na-ki na shiganta cikin NATO da Tarayyar Turai.
Gwamnatin biyu sun sami wata matsayi a Yuni a bisa wani sabon suna da suka ƙudurta, amma masu adawa na ‘yan kasanci sun yi mahawara canjin zai rage shaidar ƙabilanci na jama’a ‘yan Slav da suka yawa na Macedonia.
Shugaba Gjorge Ivanov ya ce ba zai yi zaɓe a cikin raba gardamar ba kuma wani kamfe na ƙauracewa ya sa shakku a kan ko yawan fitowar zai isa matsaikacin kashi 50 cikin ɗari da ake buƙata don raba gardamar ta inganta.
Tambayar da ke kan kuri’ar raba gardamar tana cewa: “Kai na NATO da zama mamban Tarayyar Turai ne da yarda da yarjejeniyar tare da Greece.”
Masu goyon bayan canza sunan, da suka haɗa da Firaminista Zoran Zaev, sun yi mahawara cewa wata sadaukarwa ce don bin shiga cikin hukumomin kamar su Tarayyar Turai da NATO don Macedonia, ɗaya daga cikin ƙasashe da suka bayyana daga rushewa ta Yugoslavia.
“Na zo nan yau don jefa kuri’a don makoma ta ƙasar, don mutane samari a cikin Macedonia saboda za su iya rayuwa da ‘yanci a ƙarƙashin lema ta Tarayyar Turai saboda yana nufin rayuwa mai tsaro a gare mu,” inji Olivera Georgijevska, mai shekaru 79, a cikin Skopje.
Kodayake ba ya da ƙarfi na shari’a, isassun mambobi na majalisar dokoki sun ce za su bi sakamako na jefa kuri’ar don ta zama ta daidaita.
Canza sunan zai buƙaci wan yawa na kashi biyu bisa uku na majalisar dokokin.
Hukumar zaɓe ta ƙasar ta ce babu rahotanni na matsaloli har zuwa ƙarfe 1 na rana.
Amma, fitowar ta tsaya kawai a kashi 15 cikin ɗari, idan an kwatanta da kashi 34 a cikin ɗari a zaɓen majalisar dokoki na 2016 a yayin da kashi 66 cikin ɗari na masu jefa kuri’a da ke rijista suka kaɗa kuri’arsu.
“Na fito ne don jefa kuri’a saboda ‘ya’yana, matsayinmu yana cikin Turai ne,” inji Gjose Tanevski, mai shekaru 62, wani mai jefa kuri’a cikin babban birnin, Skopje.
Firaministan Macedonia Zoran Zaev, da shi da matarsa  Zorica da ɗansa Dushko sun kaɗa kuri’arsu ta raba gardamar a cikin Macedonia a kan canza sunan ƙasar wanda zai buɗe hanya da shiga NATO da Tarayyar Turai a cikin Strumica, Macedonia 3 ga Satumba, 2018.
A gaban majalisar dokoki da ke cikin Skopje, Vladimir Kavardarkov, mai shekaru 54, ya shirya wani ƙaramin munbari kuma ya janyo kujeru sama ta gaban tanti-tanti da waɗanda ke ƙaurace wa raba gardamar suka kafa.
“Mu na NATO da Tarayyar Turai ne, amma muna son shiga da mutuncimu, ba ta bayan ƙofar aiki ba,” inji Kavadarkov.
“Mu wata ƙasa ce talaka, amma muna da kamala.
Idan ba su son su ɗauke mu a matsayin Macedonia, za mu iya juyawa ga sauran kamar China da Rusha kuma mu zama ɓangare na haɗewar Turai da Asiya.”
Firaminista Zaev ya ce zama mamban NATO zai kawo zuba jari sosai zuwa ga Macedonia, wadda ke da wani kimar rashin aikin yi na fiye da kashi 20 cikin ɗari.
“Na yi imani da yawa sosai za su so saboda fiye da kashi 80 cikin ɗari na ‘yan ƙasarmu suna son Tarayyar Turai da NATO,”inji Zaev bayan kaɗa kuri’arsa.
Ya ce wani sakamako na “eh” zai zama tabbatarwa da makomarmu.”
Wani zaɓen jin ra’ayin jama’a da Cibiyar Nazarin Ƙuduri ta Macedonia ta buga ranar Litinin ya ce tsakanin kashi 30 zuwa 43 cikin ɗari na masu jefa kuri’a za su shiga cikin raba gardamar - kasa da fitowar da ake buƙatar.
Wani jin ra’ayin jama’ar, da gidan talabijin na Telma na Macedonia, ya samo kashi 57 cikin ɗari na masu martanin suna shirya jefa kuri’ar ranar Lahadi.
Daga waɗannan, kashi 70 cikin ɗari za su so su jefa eh.
Don raba gardamar ta ci nasara da buƙatar fitowar ta zama kashi 50 cikin ɗari da ƙarin kuri’a ɗaya.
Wata gazawa a cikin raba gardamar za ta zama matsala ta farko ga ƙudurin masu goyon bayan gwamnatin Yamma tun da ta kama ragama a cikin Mayu na shekarar da ta wuce.
Kalli: Sergio Aguero na Manchester City ya kewaya ta cikin tsaro na Brighton gaba ɗaya don ci
Sergio Aguero da Raheem Sterling sun tura tsaro na  Brighton a cikin cin Manchester City 2 da 0 ranar Asabar a Filin Wasa na Etihad da ke cikin Manchester, Ingila.

Daga nan Aguero ya sami kansa a kewaye da riguna koraye huɗu.
Ya tura a kewaye da mai tsaro daya kafin gujewa sauran a gefen akwati na Brighton.
Daga nan ya tura wata miƙawa zuwa ga damansa, inda ya sami Sterling.
Ɗan wasan gaba na Ingilan ya yi amfani da tabinsa na farko a cikin akwatin don ba da ƙwallo ga Aguero, wanda ya yi amfani da takalminsa na dama don bugan golan Brighton  Mathew Ryan da wani ɗan duka zuwa cikin gefen dama na ragar.

Mun yi nasara ya yi nasarar wani ci a wannan lokacin.”

Shugaban ya ɗan ambaci yanayin da ke kewaye da wanda ya zaɓa don Kotun Koli Brett Kavanaugh a lokacin da yake magana game da amfanin fitowa ta ‘yan jam’iyyar Republican a cikin zaɓuɓɓukan tsakiyar zango.
