Jakadan Amurka ya zargi kasar Sin da 'cin zarafi' tare da 'farfaganda talla'
A mako daya bayan wata jarida ta kasar Sin ta yi amfani da shafuka hudu a kowace rana tana tallar kushe alakar kasuwanci Amurka - Sin, duk da haka, jakadun Amurka na kasar Sin ya zargi Beijing da yin amfani da manema labaran Amurka da yada farfaganda.
Amurka Shugaban kasar Donald Trump a ranar Laraba da ta gabata ya nuna cewa Sin na biyan kudi a kullum ga ragista Des Moines - Jarida mafi yawan sayarwa a Jihar Iowa - bayan da aka zarge kasar Sin da neman shiga harkokin a zaben shugaban kasa na watan Nuwamba 6, zargin da Sin ta karyata.
Zargin Trump akan cewa Beijing tana kokarin neman shiga harkokin a zaben Amurka wanda ya nuna cewa jami'an Amurka sun shaida wa kamfanin dillancin labarun Reuters cewa, wani sabon shiri ne na Washington da Amurka ta matsa lamba kan kasar Sin.
Daidai ne ga gwamnatocin kasashen waje su gabatar da tallace-tallace don inganta cinikayya, Beijing da Washington su na kulle a cikin wani yunkurin cinikayyar yaki wanda ya kai su ga matakan jadawalin kudaden shiga akan kowane.
Martanin kasar Sin na farkon akan jadawalin kuɗin fito a yakin kasuwanci shi ne kaddamar da masana'antu da za su karya jihohi irin su Iowa wanda dake goyon bayan Jam'iyyar Republican Party na Trump, Sinanci da Amurka suka fada.
Terry Branstad, jakadan Amurka a kasar Sin da kuma tsohon gwamnan jihar Iowa, babban mai sayar da kayan aikin noma zuwa kasar Sin, ya ce Beijing ta cutar da ma'aikatan Amurka, manoma da kasuwanni.
Sin, Branstad ya rubuta a wani sashi na ra'ayi a ranar Lahadi cikin Ragista Des Moines, "yanzu yana raguwar a kan wannan cin zarafi ta hanyar yin amfani da tallace-tallacen farfaganda a cikin jaridun kyauta."
"A cikin watsa labaran furofaganda, gwamnatin kasar Sin tana ba da gudummawa game da kirkirar al'adun Amurka na ‘yancin magana da ‘yancin yan jaridu ta hanyar biyan tallace-tallace a cikin Ragista Des Moines," in ji Branstad.
Ya kara da cewar, "a gurin karatu a birnin Beijing, za ku samu ba hayaniyar muryoyi da zai iya hanaku fahimtar ra’ayoyi daban-daban da al'ummar kasar Sin ke fuskanta na damuwar tatalin arziki, saboda gidan watsa labarai na karkashin ikon Jam'iyyar Kwaminis ta Sin, "in ji shi.
Ya kara da cewa "daya daga cikin jaridu mafi shahara a kasar Sin ya yi watsi da tayin don buga" labarinsa, duk da dai bai fadi wace jarida ce ba.
'Yan Republican Su na Rarraba Kan Mata Masu Zabe Gabanin Tsaka-Tsakin Mulki Tare da Kavanaugh Debacle, Masu sa ido sunyi gargadin
Da yawa daga cikin manya Republican sun tsaya kyam kuma su na kare wakilin Kotun Koli Brett Kavanaugh yayin da yake fuskantar zargin cin zarafin mata, masu sa ido sun yi gargadin cewa za su ga cikas, musamman daga mata, a lokacin zaɓen a tsaka-tsaki mai zuwa.
Halin da ke kewaye da wannan ya kasance mai girma, kuma yawancin 'yan Jamhuriyyar Republican su na cikin tsarin dake nuna cewa su na son ci gaba da zabe.
Waɗannan abubuwa ba za a iya komawa baya da su ba, "Grant Reeher, farfesa a kimiyyar siyasa a makarantar Maxwell School a Jami'ar Syracuse ya shaidawa The Hill na wani labarin da aka buga a ranar Asabar.
Reeher ya ce yana shakkun Sanata Jeff Flake na (R-Arizona) a turawan karshe na binciken FBI zai iya tunzurawa zuwa ga fushin masu zabe.
"Mata ba za su manta da abin da ya faru a jiya ba - ba za su manta da gobe ba a watan Nuwamba," in ji Karine Jean-Pierre, babban jami'in shawara kuma kakakin mai magana da yawun mata 'yan kungiyar MatsaGaba tace a ranar Jumma'a, a cewar Jaridar Washington DC.
A safiyar Jumma'a, masu zanga-zangar sun yi waka "Nuwamba na zuwa!" kamar yadda suka nuna a zauren majalisar dattawa kamar yadda 'yan Republican waɗanda ke kula da kwamitin Shari'a sun zabi su cigaba da gabatarwar Kavanaugh duk da shaidar Dr. Christine Blasey Ford, Mic ne ya kawo rohoton.
"Sha'awar dimokuradiya da karfafa gwiwa zai fita a cikin sakon," in ji Stu Rothenberg, mai ba da rahotannin siyasa, ya fada shafin labaran yanar gizon.
"Mutane su na cewa ya riga ya kasance a sama, wannan gaskiya ne.
Amma zai iya zama mafi girma, musamman a tsakanin kungiyoyin mata masu jefa kuri'a, a yankunan karkara da kananun masu jefa kuri'a, 'yan shekaru 18 zuwa 29, waɗanda ba su son shugaba, ba za su yi zabe ba."
Ko kafin shaida Ford ta bayyana ga jama’a game da zarginta na cin zarafin jima'i akan Kotun Koli zababbe, masu sharhi sun nuna goyon bayan da za su iya biyo baya idan Jamhuriyyar Republican ta ci gaba da tabbatarwa.
"Wannan ya zama babban rikici ga GOP," in ji Michael Steele, tsohon shugaban kwamitin Republican Kwamitin Tarayya, a farkon makon da ya gabata, a cewar Labaran NBC.
"Ba kawai game da zaben kwamitin ko zaben karshe ko kuma Kavanaugh aka sanya a kan benci, kuma game da yadda Republicans suka magance wannan da yadda suka yi mata," Guy Cecil, darektan Fifikon Amurka, wani rukuni na taimakawa don zabe 'yan Democrat, da aka nuna wa tashar watsa labarai.
Duk da haka, Amirkawa sun rabu akan wanda zasu gaskanta bayan bayyyanar shaidar Ford da Kavanaugh, tare da rinjaye kadan da kuna rinjaye anjima.
Wani sabon zabe YouGov ya nuna kashi 41 cikin dari na masu amsa shakka ko tabbas sun gaskanta gaskiyar Ford, yayin da kashi 35 cikin dari sun tabbata ko tabbas sunyi imani da Kavanaugh.
Bugu da ƙari, kashi 38 cikin dari sun ce sunyi tunanin Kavanaugh ya yi ƙarya a lokacin da yake gabatar da shaida, yayin da kawai kashi 30 cikin dari suka faɗi daidai da Ford.
Bayan turi daga Flake, FBI na binciken lamarin da Ford suka gabatar da shi tare da wani mutum daya da ake zargi, Deborah Ramirez, a cewar The Guardian.
Ford ya bayyana a gaban Majalisar kwamitin Dattijan Shari'a da rantsuwa a makon da ya wuce cewa Kavanaugh na maye lokacin da yaci zarafinta tana da shekaru 17.
Ramirez yayi zargin cewa zababben dan Kotun Kolin ya nuna al'aurarsa gare ta yayin da suke halarci wata ƙungiya a yayin da suke karatun Yale a shekarun 1980.
Wanda ya kirkiro yanar gizo ta duniya yana shirin fara sabon yanar gizo akan farfajiyar google da facebook.
Tim Berners-Lee, wanda ya Ƙirƙiri Yanar Gizo a duniya, yana ƙaddamar fara wani shiri wanda zai yi gogayya da Facebook, Amazon da Google.
Kayan aikin fasaha na zamani Inrupt, wani kamfanin ne wanda ke gina cibiyar dandalin budewa na Berners-Lee Solid.
Ma’adinai na ba masu amfani damar zabar wajen adana bayyanai da kuma abin da aka ba mutane damar samun damar bayanai.
A wata ganawa ta musamman tare da kamfanin Fast, Berners-Lee ya raha cewa, dalilin kera Inrupt shi ne "mulkin duniya."
"Ba dole ne mu yi shi yanzu ba," ya ce game da farawa.
"Lokacin tarihi ne yanzu."
Aikace-aikace yana amfani da fasaha na Solid don bawa mutane damar ƙirƙirar nasu "bayanan ajiya a intanit" ko POD.
Yakan ƙunshi jerin lambobin sadarwa, jerin abubuwan da za’a yi, kalandar, ɗakin karatu na wakoki da wasu kayan aiki na kai kadai da gwanayen kayan aiki.
Yana kama da Google Drive, Microsoft Outlook, Slack da Spotify duk su na samuwa a kan farfajiyar bincike daya duk a lokaci guda.
Abun ban mamaki game da gurbin ajiya na kai a shagon yanar gizo shi ne cewa mai amfani da shi na da cikakken ikon samun irin bayanai.
Kamfanin ya kira shi "karfafawa ta hanyar bayanan da aka tattara ."
Ra’ayin Inrupt, a cewar Shugaban kamfanin John Bruce, shi ne kamfanin zai kawo albarkatun, tsari da kuma dacewa don taimakawa wajen samar da Solid ga kowa.
Kamfanin a halin yanzu ya ƙunshi Berners-Lee, Bruce, wani tsari na tsaro wanda IBM ya saya, wasu masu haɓaka ma'aikata sun yi aiki akan aikin, da ƙungiyar ‘yan sa kan coders.
Farawa daga wannan satin, masu samar da fasaha a duniya za su iya ƙirƙirarar tasu mahanja da aka rarrabe ta hanyar amfani da kayan aikin da aka samu akan shafin Inrupt.
Berners-Lee ya bayyana cewa shi da abokansa ba su tatauna da "Facebook da Google ba game da ko za su gabatar da canji inda duk samfurin kasuwancin su za su gabata a cikin dare.
"Ba ma neman izinin su."
A cikin wata jarida da aka buga a ranar Asabar, Berners-Lee ya rubuta cewa "Inrupt" manufar shi ne samar da makamashi na kasuwanci da kuma al'amarin don taimakawa wajen kare amincin da ingancin ginin sabon shafin yanar gizon Solid. "
A 1994, Berners-Lee ya sake canza yanar-gizon lokacin da ya kafa Gammayar Duniyar Yanar Gizo a Cibiyar Fasaha Massachusetts.
A cikin 'yan watanni, Berners-Lee ya kasance mai babbar murya a cikin muhawarar rashin daidaito.
Ko da a lokacin da aka kaddamar da Inrupt, Berners-Lee zai kasance wanda ya kafa da kuma mai ba da umarni na Gammayyar Yanar Gizo, mai suna Web Foundation da Budaden Cibiyar Bayanai.
Ina da kyakyawan fata ga wannan sauyin zamani na yanar gizo, “berners -lee ya kara da cewa.
Bernard Vann: An karrama malamin WW1 victoria cross
Babban ikilisiyar chocin ingila daya taba lashe kyautar girma na Victoria cross a lokacin yakin duniya Daya kuma jajirtacce ya sha bikin murna a garin su shekaru 100 da doriya.
Lt Col The Reverend Bernard Vann ya lashe lambar yabo a ranar 29 Satumba 1918 a harin a Bellenglise da Lehaucourt.
Duk da haka, maharbin boye ne ya kashe shi kwanaki hudu daga bisani, kuma bai san cewa ya lashe kyauta mafi girma na sojojin Birtaniya ba.
An bayyana dutsen tunawa da shi wanda jikokin shi guda biyu ne suka gabatar a wani shinge a Rushden, Northamptonshire, ranar Asabar.
Ɗaya daga cikin jikokinsa, Michael Vann, ya ce "kayatacciyar alama" ce wanda za a bayyana dutsen shekaru 100 daidai da samun kyautar kakansa.
A cewar kundin tarihin London, ranar 29 ga Satumba 1918, Lt Col Vann ya jagoranci dakarunsa a fadin Canal de Saint-Quentin "ta hanyar mai matukar damuwa da hazo mai matukar duhu ga wuta daga filin daga da bindigogi na inji."
Daga bisani sai ya haura zuwa layin harbi tare "mafi girma jarumta" wanda ya jagorancin gaban layin kafin ya fakaito da bindigar -fili shi kadai kuma ya durkusa runduna uku.
Maharbin ɓoye na ƙasar Jamus ne ya kashe Laftanar Kanar Vann a ranar 4 ga watan Oktobar 1918 - wata daya kawai kafin a gama yaƙin.
Michael Vann, mai shekaru 72, ya ce ayyukan kakansa "wani abu da na san cewa ba zan taba iya zama ba sai dai wani abu da yake da tawali'u."
Shi da ɗan'uwansa, Dr James Vann, sun kuma sanya kyalle bayan faretin, wanda Brentwood Imperial Youth Band ya jagoranta.
Michael Vann ya ce "na ji daɗin karamawan sosai don rawan da na taka a cikin faratin" kuma ya kara da cewa babban jarumi ne wanda a nunawa goyon baya da kuma taimakon da mutane ke bayarwa."
Masoyan MMA sun kwana a zaune domin kallon Bellator 206, amma kuma sai suka samu Peppa Pig a maimako
Ka yi la'akari da haka, ka kwana zaune don kallon Bellator 206 amma kawai sai a hana ka kallon ainihin taron.
Lissafin daga San Jose ya ƙunshi fadace-fadace 13, ciki harda shida a kan babban katin kuma an nuna su kai tsaye cikin dare a Birtaniya akan Tasha na 5.
Ƙarfe 6 na safe, kamar yadda Gegard Mousasi da Rory MacDonald suka shirya don fuskantar juna, masu kallo a Birtaniya sun kasance masu mamaki lokacin da yanayin ya canza zuwa Peppa Pig.
Wadansu ba su damu ba bayan sun kwana zaune har zuwa har farkon safiya musamman don fadan.
Masoyi daya ya bayyana a Twitter cewa canji zuwa zane mai ban dariya na yara kamar “wani irin wasan mararsa lafiya.’
"Dokar gwamnati ce cewa karfe 6 na safe a canza tashar domin shirin bai dace ba don haka dole su canza zuwa shirye shiryen yara," in ji Dave Schwartz, matamakin shugaba na sadarwa da kasuwanci, lokacin da aka tambaye shi game da watsawa.
""Peppa aleden," eh."
Shugaban kamfanin Bellator, Scott Coker, ya ce za su yi aiki a kan shirye-shiryen su hade da masu kallo na Birtaniya a nan gaba.
"Ina tsammanin idan na yi tunani game da sake bugawa, ina tsammanin zai iya wadatarwa," in ji Coker.
"Amma shida ne na safiyar ranar Lahadi a can, kuma ba za mu iya yin hakan ba har sai lokacin mu na Lahadi, Litinin lokacin su.
amma mu na aiki akan shi.
Ku yarda da ni, lokacin da aka sauya shi a can akwai sakonni da suke ta yawo gaba da baya kuma dukansu ba su da dadi.
Mu na ƙoƙarin gyara shi, mun yi tsammani abu ne da ya shafi matsalar fasaha.
Amma ba haka ba, batu ne na gwamnati.
Ina maku alkwalin hakan ba zai sake faruwa ba.
Ku yarda dani, lokacin da aka sauya shi a can akwai sakonni da suke ta yawo gaba da baya kuma dukansu ba su da dadi.
halin takaici ne.”
Hamada Tsibirin Discs: Tom Daley ya ji 'dagawa' saboda jinsi
Ɗan wasan Olympics Tom Daley ya ce ya girma yana jin dagawa fiye da kowa saboda jinsin sa - amma hakan ne ya bashi hazaka wajen samun nasara.
Dan shekaru 24 ya ce bai fahimta ba har sai da ya tafi makarantar sakandare cewa "ba kowa ba ne kamar ni."
Da yake jawabi a gidan farko Rediyo 4 Hamadan Tsibiri wanda Lauren Laverne ya gabatar, ya ce ya yi magana game da hakkokin 'yan luwadi na ba da wasu "fata".
Kuma yace kasancewarsa uba ya sanya shi rashin damuwa akan cin wasan Olympics.
Mai gabatarwa da shirin na yau da kullum, Kirsty Young, ya dauki watanni da dama na hutu saboda rashin lafiya.
Yayin da ya bayyana a matsayin wani na daban a kan shirin farko na Laverne, Daley ya ce yana jin "kasa da" kowa na girma saboda "ba a yarda da ba jama’a su so maza da 'yan mata ba."
Ya ce: "Har wa yau, irin abubuwan da nake ji na ƙasa da, da kuma jin wani abu daban, sun kasance ainihin abubuwan da suka ba ni iko da karfi don samun nasara."
Ya so ya tabbatar da cewa shi "wani abu," in ji shi, don haka bai yi takaici ga kowa ba a lokacin da suka gano jinsin sa.
Wakilin wasan Olympics na tagulla guda biyu ya zama dan wasan LGBT mai girma kuma ya yi amfani da shi a gasar Commonwealth na wannan shekara a Australia don neman kara yawan kasashe da zasu bada daman luwadi.
Ya ce ya yi magana ne saboda ya ji daɗin kasancewa a fili ba tare da raguwa ba kuma yana so ya ba wasu "fata".
Shi zakara uku a duniya ya ce fadawa soyaya da namij i-dan wasan Dustin Lance Black na Amurka, wanda ya hadu da shi a 2013 - "ya zame man abun mamaki."
Daley ya auri zakaran Oscar, wanda ya girme shi da shekaru 20, a bara amma ya ce tazarar shekarun ba damuwa bane.
"Idan kayi fama da abubuwa da yawa a kanana shekaru" - ya tafi wasan Olympics din shi na farko yana da shekaru 14 kuma mahaifinsa ya mutu ciwon daji bayan shekaru uku - ya ce yana da wuya a sami mutumin da ya taɓa samun irin wannan matsayi sama da kasa.
Ma’auratan sun zama iyaye a Yuni, ga ɗa mai suna Robert Ray Black-Daley, kuma Daley ya ce “dukka haganen zaman gaban shi” ya canja.
“Idan da ka tambayeni bara, duk batun ‘ina bukatan na ci lambar zinariya ne’, inji shi.
“Ka san meye, akwai wasu manyan abubuwa fiye da lambar zinariyar wasar Olympics.
Lambar zinariyar wasar Olympics dina Robbie ne.”
Dan shi yana da suna daya da baban shi Robert, wanda ya mutu a 2011 a shekara 40 bayan an gano shi da cutar daji ta kwakwalwa.
Daley ya ce baban shi bai yarda cewa zai mutu ba kuma abun daya daga cikin abubuwan karshe da ya tambaya shi ne idan su na da tiketin su zuwa Landan 2012 - tun da yana son ya zauna a layin gaba.
“Ban iya ce mashi ‘ba zaka samu daman zama a layin gaba ba baba’,” ya ce.
“Ina rike da hannun shi a lokacin da ya daina nunfashi kuma har sai da ya asalin daina numfashi kuma ya mutu kafin na yarda cewa dan Adam ne,” ya ce.
Shekarar gaban Daley ya yi takara a wasar Olympics na 2012 kuma ya ci tagulla.
“Ni kawai na san cewa wannan shi ne abun da nake mafarkin shi duk rayuwa ta - na yi iyo a gaban taron mutanen gida a Wasar Olympics, babu wani yanayi da yafi haka,” ya ce.
Kuma yayi wahayi a zabin wakar shi ta farko - Alfahari daga Heather Small - wanda yayi jimame da shi a shirye shiryen wasar Olympics kuma ya ke tayar mashi da sigar jiki.

An ajiye gajiyayyen dan wasa Mickelson a gasar Kofin Ryder ranar Asabar
Dan wasan Amurka Phil Mickelson zai kafa tarihi a ranar Lahadi lokacin da ya taka leda a gasar cin kofin Ryder na 47, amma dole ne ya sauya tsarinsa don kauce baƙin ciki a matsayin.
Mickelson, wanda ke taka leda a cikin biki na 12, kyaftin Jim Furyk ne ya ajiye dan wasan a kwallo hudu ga mutum hudu na ranar Asabar.
Maimakon kasancewarsa a tsakiyar wasan, kamar yadda ya saba wa Amurka, fitaccen mai nasara sau biyar ya raba ranar tsakaninsa na kasancewa mai karfafawa da kuma aiki a kan wasansa a kan layi tare da bege na gyara abin da yake da shi .
Bai kasance tsayayye cikin deribobi ba ko a lokacin tashen wasan sa, dan shekaru 48 bai dace ba ga matakin wasan tsukakken wasan Le Golf na filin Tarayya, inda ke da tsayi ga azabtarwa da mummunar tashin hankali.
Kuma idan wasan da kansa bai dace ba, Mickelson, a wasan na tara a ranar Lahadi, ya fuskanci babban zakara na Birtaniya Francesco Molinari, wanda ya haɗe tare da rookie Tommy Fleetwood don lashe dukkanin wasanni hudu a wannan makon.
Idan mutanen amurka, da maki hudu kasa sun nuna cewa za su fara wasanni daidaiku 12, su tashi da zafi zuwa fara wasa, wasan na Mickelson zai zama mai muhimmiyar mahimmanci.
Furyk ya nuna amincewa da mutumin na shi, duk da ba zai iya cewa komai ba kuma.
"Ya fahimci muhimmancin da yake da ita a yau, ya tattaɓani a baya kuma ya sanya hannunsa kewaye da ni, ya ce zai kasance a shirye gobe," inji Furyk.
"Ya amince da kanshi sosai.
Yana cikin sanannen jarumai kuma an karu da shi sosai a wannan kungiyar a da, kuma da wannan satin.
Ban taɓa tsammanin zai yiwu ya buga wasani biyu ba.
Na yi tsammanin fiye, amma haka tsarin ya ke kuma itace hanyar da mu ke tunanin za mu bi.
Ya so ya kasance a can waje, kamar sauran mutane. "
Mickelson zai wuce tarihin Nick Faldo a gasar cin kofin Ryder da aka buga ranar Lahadi.
Zai iya kawo ƙarshen wasan Ryder Cup wanda ba zai taɓa misaltuwa ba da babban matakin tarihin shi kadai.
Mickelson ya ci wasanni 18, an ci shi 20 da kuma sun zuze a bakwai, duk da cewa Furyk ya ce kasancewarsa ya kawo wasu abubuwan mahimmai ga kungiyar.
"Yana da ban dariya,wauta, mai ƙayatarwa, yana da son zolayar mutane, kuma ya zama babban dan wasa a cikin dakin wasan," inji shi.
"Ina tsammanin matasan ‘yan wasa na son zolayar shi, har ma, wannan satin, abin da yake da ban sha'awa.
Ya kawo abubuwa da yawa fiye da wassani kawai.”
Kyaftin din Turai Thomas Bjorn ya san bada babban tazara zai shuɗe ba da daɗewa ba
Thomas Bjorn, kyaftin din Turai, ya sani daga kwarewa sa cewa samun tazara kadan a cikin 'yan kwanaki na karshe a wasan daidaiku na Ryder Cup zamewa tuki ma wahala.
Dane ya fara bugawa wasan shi na farko a 1997 a Valderrama, inda Seve Ballesteros ke jagorantar da maki biyar a kan 'yan Amurkan amma dai kawai ya sami nasarar kammala layi tare da hancunan su a gaba a tazarar mafi karanta, inda ya lashe 14½- 13½.
"Ka ci gaba da tunatar da kanka cewa mu na da babban jagora a Valderrama, mu na da babban jagora a Brookline, inda muka rasa, kuma a Valderrama, inda muka ci nasara, amma kawai," inji Bjorn, wanda ya kwatanta, bayan kallon Ajin 2018 lashe 5-3 a ranar Jumma'a da kuma jiya don kai 10-6 a Le Golf National.
Toh Tarihi zai nuna mani da duk wanda ke wannan kungiyar cewa ba’a gama ba tukun.
Kana da cikaken shiga gobe.
ka je can kayi duka abun da ya kamata daidai.
Ba’a gama wannan ba sai ka samo makunan dake kan allo.
Mu na da manufa, kuma shi ne mu kokarta muci wannan kofin, kuma nan ne inda zamu mai da himma.
Na fada tun farko, ina mai da himma akan ‘yan wasa 12 dake tawagarmu, amma kuma duk mun san mai ke faruwa a dayan ɓangaren - su na da zakarun yan wasa na duniya.”
Sanin yadda wadannan ‘yan wasan suka yi a filin golf mai wahala, Bjorn ya kara: “Ba zan taɓa zuwa sama da kaina ba a wannan.
Gobe na daban ne babba.
Gobe shi ne yin daidaiku da ke zuwa gaba, kuma shima abu ne na daban wajen yi.
Yana da kyau idan ya kasance tare da abokin tarayya lokacin da abubuwa ke da kyau, amma idan kun fita waje ɗaidaiku, to ana jarraba ku da cikakken ikon ku a matsayin golfer.
Wannan shi ne saƙo da kake buƙatar ya isa zuwa ga 'yan wasa, shi ne fitar da iya kwazon ka gobe.
Yanzu, ku bar abokanku a baya domin dole ne fitar da iya kwazon sa da kanshi, da kuma. "
Ya bambanta da Bjorn, kishiyar lambar Jim Furyk zai nemi 'yan wasansa suyi aiki da kwarewa fiye da yadda suke yi a tarayya, waɗanda suka hada da Jordan Spieth da Justin Thomas, wanda ya dauki maki uku daga cikin hudu.
Furyk kansa ya kasance a kan iyakar wadannan manyan rukuni na baya-bayan nan, bayan kasancewa daya daga cikin 'yan wasan da suka lashe gasar a Brookline kafin su ci gaba da hasara yayin da Turai ta cire "Miracle a Madinah."
"Ina tunawa da duk wani mummunar magana," in ji shi a amsa cewa ana tambayar shi yadda Ben Crenshaw, kyaftin din a shekarar 1999, ya haɗa 'yan wasansa zuwa ranar ƙarshe.
"Mu na da wasanni 12 gobe, amma kuma sai kun tashi fara zuwa da sauri kamar yadda kuka gani a Brookline, kamar yadda kuka gani a Medinah.
Lokacin da damuwa ya shiga ta hanya ɗaya, yana sanya matsanancin matsa lamba a kan waɗannan wassanin tsakiyar.
Mun kafa matakanmu bisa ga yadda ya kamata kuma muka sanya mutanen su cikin salon da muke so, kun sani, mu na ƙoƙarin yin bada mamaki a gobe. "
An baiwa Thomas damar kokarin jagorancin Rory McIlroy a wasan sama tare da Paul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommy Fleetwood da Ian Poulter da sauran 'yan Turai a cikin rabin sama a wannan tsarin.
"Na tafi tare da wannan rukuni na mutane a cikin wannan tsari domin ina ganin yana rufe duk hanyar," in ji Bjorn na zabukansa.
An sake jinkirta sabon jirgin yakin ruwa Jamus kuma
Ya kamata a kaddamar da sabon jirgin Sojin ruwan Jamus a shekarar 2014 don maye gurbin jiragen yaki tsofaffi Sanyi na zamani yaki. amma ba zai kasance ba har sai a kalla a shekara ta gaba saboda kuskuren tsarin da farashin dusar ƙanƙara, rahotanni na kafofin watsa labaru sun ruwaito.
Kadamar da Rheinland-Pfalz, wadda ke jagorantar sabon nauyin Baden-Wuerttemberg, yanzu an dakatar da shi har zuwa farkon rabin shekarar 2019, in ji wata sanarwa ta Die Zeit.
Ya kamata jirgin ya shiga Rundunar Sojan ruwa a shekarar 2014, amma matsalolin kamin kawowa ya tsaida da rabon zakulalen aikin.
Jiragen ruwa hudu na Baden-Wuerttemberg da Sojin ruwa suka bada salahun a 2007 zai zo ne a matsayin sauyi ga tsohon Bremen-class frigates.
An fahimci cewa za su ƙunshi wata tashar wuta mai karfi, jigon kayan yaki na jiragen sama da na jirgin ruwa da wasu fasahar zamani, kamar rage radar, infrared da kuma sa hannun sauti.
Wasu muhimman siffofi sun haɗa da tsawon lokaci na haɓakawa - ya kamata a yi amfani da sabon frigates har zuwa shekaru biyu daga tashoshin ruwan gida.
Duk da haka, kara jinkirin yana nuna ingancin jirgin yaƙin - wanda zai ba Jamus izinin malakar karfin yaki a saman teku - zasu zama sun fita yayi a lokacin da za su shiga hidima, bayanin Die Zeit.
Aibun F125 Frigate ya zama babban labari a shekarar bara, lokacin da jami’an sojin ruwa na Jamus suka ki kaddamar da jirgin kuma suka mayar da su zuwa wajen ajiyar Blohm & Voss a Hamburg.
Wanna shi ne karin farka da Sojin ruwa zai mayar da jirgi zuwa ga mai gina shi bayan ya isar.
Kadan aka sani game da dalilan da suka sa aka mayar, amma kafofin watsa labaru na Jamus sun ba da labarin "lahani da manhaja" wanda suka sa jirgin yakin zai zame marar amfani idan an tura shi a aikin gwagwarmaya.
Karancin Manhaja ya kasance mai muhimmiyar muhimmanci kamar yadda ma'aikatan jirgin ruwa 120 na Baden-Wuerttemberg ke gudanar da su. Kusan rabin ma'aikatan tsohon Bremen class frigates.
Har ila yau, ya bayyana cewa jirgin yana da nau’in mai nauyi wanda ya rage yin aikinsa kuma ya ƙayyade ikon sojin ruwa ingantawa na gaba.
An kiyasta cewa "Rheinland-Pfalz" na ton 7,000 "yana da nauyi a matsayin jiragen ruwa na irin wannan jirgi da Jamus ke amfani da ita a yakin duniya na biyu.
Baya ga kayan aiki mara kyau, farashin dukan aikin - ciki har da horar da ma'aikatan - yana zama batun.
An ce an kai kimanin dala biliyan €3.1 ($ 3.6bn) - daga farkon biliyan €2.2.
Matsalolin da ke damun sabbin frigates sun zama mahimmanci a fagen gargadi na baya-bayan nan cewa ikon jiragen ruwa na Jamus yana raguwa.
Tun da farko wannan shekara, Hans-Peter Bartels, babban kwamandan kwamitin tsaro na kasar Jamus, ya amince da cewa jirgin ruwa na hakika yana "jiragen ruwa ya fara fita lokacin kaddamarwa na-jirage masu dama."
Jami'in ya ce matsalar ta dusar ƙanƙara a kan lokaci, saboda an dakatar da manyan jiragen ruwa tsofaffi amma ba a ba a kawo masu mayewa ba.
Ya yi baƙin ciki cewa babu wani daga cikin 'yan Baden-Wuerttemberg da suka shiga cikin jirgin ruwa.
Tarayya Aminci na leken asirin rayuwar jemagu
Sabon binciken da ake yi a wani yankin gidajen Sama na Scottish yana da manufa bayyana yadda jemagu suke amfani da wuri a cikin farauta don abinci.
Ana fatan sakamakon binciken zai bayar da sabon haske game da halayyar mammals masu tashi da kuma taimakawa wajen jagorancin ayyukan kiyayewa na gaba.
Masana binciken da masanan kimiyya suka yi a Tarrayan Aminci na Scotland za su bi na kullun da soprano pipistrelles tare da launin ruwan kasa da dogon-kunne da jamagen Daubenton a cikin Inverewe Gardens a Wester Ross.
za’a sanya naurar daukar murya na musamman a wajeje daban a zagayen kayayyakin domin duba al’amorin jemagun a cikin dukkan kakan.
Ma’aikatan NHS da masu sa kai za su kuma gudanar da bincike na wayar tafi-da-gidanka ta yin amfani da bincike na hannun.
Sakamakon sautin daga kwararru na dukkan daukan muryan za su iya sa a gane yawan kiran jemagu kuma da abin da kowane jinsuna ke yi.
Za a samar da taswira da rahoto na al'ada don ƙirƙirar hoto mai zurfi game da halin su.
Rob Dewar, mai ba da shawara game da yanayin na NTS, yana fatan sakamakon zai bayyana abin da yankunan zama mafi muhimmanci ga jemagui da kuma yadda suke amfani da kowannensu.
Wannan bayani zai taimaka wajen ƙayyade amfani da aikin gudanarwa na gida kamar aikin samar da kayan aiki da kuma yadda zai fi dacewa don kula da gandun daji na jemagu da wasu irin jinsuna su.
Yawan jemagu a Scotland da wasu kasashen Bitaniya ya sauka sosai a cikin karni na baya.
Su na cikin barazana daga gine-gine da aikin ci gaba da ke shafar hawaye da asarar wurin zama.
Hasken iska da hasken lantarki na iya haifar da haɗari, kamar yadda jaridu da wasu magungunan sunadarai na kayan gine-gine suke yi, da kuma hare-haren daga dabba gida maguna.
Gaskiyar shi ne jemgai ba makafai bane.
Duk da haka, saboda halin su na farautan dare kunnuwan su sun fi amfani bisa ga idanuwansu idan yazo batun kama nama.
Su na amfani da haddaden tsarin sauraren sautin wuri da gano kwari da abubuwan dake tashe hanyar su.
NTS, waɗanda ke da nauyin kiyaye fiye da gidanjen tarii 270, lambuna masu amfani 38 da kadada 76,000 na fili a cikin kasar, su na daukan jemage da matukan mahimmanci.
Yana da kwarraru goma, masu yawan yin bincike, dibin tarin gidajen jemagai da kuma ceto wani lokaci.
Masana’antar ta ma bude gidan ajiyar jemagai kawai na farko a Scotland a Dukiyar Threave dake Dumfires da Galloway, wanda ke da jinsi jemagai 8 daga cikin goma na Scotland.
Manajan Dukiyar David Thompson yace dukiyar na yanki mafi dacewa masu.
“Nan a Threave mu na da kyakkyawan yanki wa jemagai,” yace.
“Mu na da tsofaffin gidaje, tsoffafin itace da kuma mazauni mai kyau.
Amma akwai abubuwa da yawa akan jemagai da ba a sani ba, saboda haka ayyukan da muke yi akan wannan dukiyar zai taimake mu wajen gane wasu abubuwa da suke bukata dan su bunƙasa.”
Ya jaddada mahimmanci diba jenmagan kafin a yi aikin kulawa da dukiyar tunda yana yiyuwa rusa tarin gidan matan zai iya kai ga mutuwan har matan su da yaran su 400, wanda zai iya yiyuwar shafe gaba ki daya yawan tsuntsayen yankin.
Ana kiyaye jemagai dan haka bai hallatta a kashe su, tayar masu da hankali ko damuwar su ko rigiza gidajen su ba.
Elisabeth Ferrel, Jami’ar Scotland ta Ma’aikatar Kula da Jemage, ta nemi goyon bayan mutane su hada gwiwa wurin taimakawa.
Ta ce: “Mu na da abubuwa da yawa da zamu koya akan jemagai da kuma jinsunan su masu yawa kwai bamu san yadda yanayin yawan su yake ba.”
Ronaldo yayi watsi da ikirarin fyaɗe a yayin da lauyoyi suke shirin su kai ƙarar mujallar Jamus.
Cristiano Ronaldo yayi kira da ikirarin da aka mashi akan fyaɗe akan “labarun ƙarya”, yana cewa mutane “su na so su inganta kansu” ta hanyar amfani da sunan shi.
Lauyoyin shi su na shirin kai ƙarar mujallar Jamus Der Spiegel, wanda suka buga zargin.
An zargi dan wasan gaban na Portugal da Juventus da yi wa wata mata ‘yar Amurka fyaɗe, mai suna Kathryn Mayorga, a wani dakin otel na Las Vegas a 2009.
Ana zargin cewa bayan haka ya biya ta dala 375,000 dan ta rufe bakin ta akan abun, Der Spiegel sun yi rihoto ranar Jumma’a.
A lokacin da yake magana ta hanyar bidiyon shi ta Instagram da masu bin shi Miliyan 142 sa’o’i bayan an yi rihoton ikirarin, Ronaldo, 33, yayi watsi da rihoton matsayin “labarin karya”
“A’a, a’a, a’a, a’a, a’a.
abun da suka ce yau, labarin karya ne,” maciyin Ballon d’Or biyar din yace a cikin kamarar.
“Su na so su inganta kansu ta hanyar amfani da suna na.
Hakan daidai ne.
Su na so su yi suna ta hanyar ambaton suna na, amma yana cikin aikin.
“Ni mutun ne dake cikin kwanciyar hankali kuma komai kalau,” dan wasan ya ƙara, yana murmushi.
Lauyoyi masu kare Ronaldo su na shirin su kai ƙarar Der Spiegel akan zargin, wanda suka kira “Rihoton da bashi da hujja akan zargi ta yankin sirri,” bisa ga Reuters.
Lawyer Christian Schertz ya ce dan wasan zai nemi cin tara akan “ɓata masa halaye na dabi'a, a cikin adadin da ya dace da nauyin laifin, wanda yakan iya zama mafi tsananin cin zarafin haƙin ɗan adam a cikin shekarun nan.”
Zargin ana cewa wai ya faru ne a Yuni 2009 a wani babban ɗaki na Palm Otel and Casino a Las Vegas.
Bayan sun hadu a wani gidan wasan kwaikwayo na dare, Ronaldo da Mayorga wai sun koma dakin dan wasan, wurin da a zargin ya mata fyaɗe a duburi, bisa ga takardun da aka saka a fayil ɗin dake Kotun Gundumar Clark a Nevada.
Mayorga tayi ikirari cewa Ronaldo ya faɗi akan gwiwan shi bayan hakan kuma ya ce mata “kashi 99” “mutumin kirki” wanda ke samun akasi daga “kashi ɗaya”.
Takardur su na ikirari cewa Ronaldo ya gasganta cewa su biu sun yi jima’i, amma cikin yarjejeniya ce.
Mayorga kuma tayi ikirari cewa ta je wajen ‘yan sanda kuma an ɗauki hotunan raunin da ta ji a asibit, amma daga baya ta yadda da sulhu a wajen kotu saboda ta ji “tsoron ramuwa” kuma ta damu akan “dizguwa a fuskar mutane.”
Yar shekara 34 ɗn yanzu tana neman juya sulhun a yayin da ta ci gaba da fuskantar kunci daga abun da ya farun.
Ronaldo yana kan komawa Real Madrid daga Manchester United a lokacin da farmakin da ake zargin ya faru, kuma wannan ranin ya koma babban kungiyar kwallon Italia Juventus a yarjejeniyar Yuro miliyan100.
Brexit: UK ‘har abada zata yi da na sanin’ rasa masu kera motoci
UK “zata yi da na sanin shi har abada” idan tayi rashin matsayin ta na shugabancin kera mota bayan Brexit, Sakataren Sana’a Greg Clark yace.
Ya kara cewa abun “damuwa ne” cewa Toyota UK ta fada wa BBC cewa idan Britain ta fita EU ba tare da yarjejeniya ba zata sayar da aiki na dan wani lokaci a masana’antar ta a Burnaston, kusa da Derby.
“Mu na bukatar yarjejeniya,” Mr Clark ya ce.
Kamfanin Japan din na mota yace tasirin jinkiri a iyakar kasa a yanayin Brexit babu yarjejeniya zai iya kwao rasa ayyuka.
Masana’antar Burnaston din - wanda ke hada Toyota Auris da Avensis - sun kera kusan motoci 150,000 bara wanda a ciki kashi 90 aka fitar zuwa sauran kasashen Turai.
“A gani na shi ne idan Britain ta fita EU a karshen Maris zamu ga sayawar kira a masana;antar mu,” inji Mavin Cooke, Manajin Direkta na Toyota a Burnaston.
Wasu masu kera motocin UK sun nuna jin tsoro akan fita EU ba tare da yarjejniya ba akan yadda kasuwancin tsallaken iyaka zai kasance, har da Honda, BMW da Jaguar Land Rover.
BMW, kamar misali, ta ce zata kulle karamin masana’antar ta da ke Oxford na tsawon wata daya bayan Brexit.
Babban damuwan yana dangance da abun da makera motoci suka ce ne dangane da hadarin samun kayayyakin aiki idan akayi Brexit ba yarjejeniya.
Ana aiwatar da hanyar sarrafawar Toyota na akan tsarin “gab-da-lokaci”, yadda sassa su na isowa ko wani minti 37 daga masu kaya duk daga UK da EU na motocin da ake kira dan sari.
Idan UK ta bar EU ba tare dayarjejeniya ba ranar 29 ga watan Maris, za’a iya samun matsaloli a iyaka wanda masana’antar ta ce yakan iya kawo jinkiri da rashin isashen sassa.
Ba zai yiyu Toyota ta rike fiye da kayan aiki na kwana daya a masana’antar ta na Derbyshire, kamfanin ta ce, dan haka aiki zai saya.
Mr Clark ya ce tsarin binciken Theresa May na dagantakan gaba da EU an “asalin tsara shi dan kauyce wa wadannan binciken a iyaka.”
“Mu na bukatar mu samu yarjejeniya. Mu na so mu samu mafi kyakkyawan yarjejeniya da zai bamu daman kamar yadda na fada ba kawai nasaran da zamu ji dadin shi a halin yanzu ba amma mu samu yin amfani da wannan daman,” ya fada a tsarin Yau na Radiyon BBC 4.
“Hujjan da ba na Toyota ba kawai amma har da na wasu makera shi ne mu na asalin bukatar mu ci gaba da abun da yake nasarraren samar da kayaki.”
Toyota ta kasa fadan tsawon lokacin da za a sayar da aiki, amma a hangen gaba, sun bada gargadin cewa farashi zai rage karfin gasar masana’antar kuma hakan zai kai ga asarar ayyuka.
Peter Tsouvallaris, wanda yayi aiki a Burnaston na tsawon shekaru 24 kuma shi ne kakakin kungiyar hadin kai a masana’antar, yace mambobin su na ci gaba da damuwa: “A cikin kwarewata da zaran wadannan ayyukan sun tafi ba sa taba dawowa.
Wani kakakin gwamnati ya ce: “Mun mika tsarin daidai kuma na gaskiya don alakar mu ta gaba da EU.”
Haduwar Trump da Rosenstein zai iya samun jinkiri kuma, inji White House
Haduwar Donald Trump na mahimmanci da mataimakin lauya janar Rod Rosenstein zai iya “matsawa gaba da sati daya” a yayin da fada akan waklin babban kotu Brett Kavanaugh ya ci gaba, White House ta ce ranar Lahadi.
Rosenstein ke kula da aikin mashawarci na musamman Robert Mueler, wanda ke binciken tsangwamar Rasha akan zabe, mahadi tsakanin ma’aikatan Trump da Russia da yiyuwar toshe adalci daga Shugaban kasar.
Shin Trump zai kori ko ba zai kori mataimakin alkalin alkalai daga aiki, a hakan ya saka ‘yancin Mueller cikin hadari, ya cika gulmar Washington a watanni.
Farkon watan nan, New York Times sun yi rihoto cewa Rosenstein ya tattauna tare da waya dan rikodin labarin shi da Trump da kuma yiyuwar cire Shugaban kasar ta hanyar doka a 25.
Rosenstein ya karyata rihoton.
Amma Litinin din da ta wuce ya je White House, a cikin rahoton cewa zai yi marabus.
A maimakon haka, haduwar shi da Trump, wanda a lokacin yake Majalisar Dinkin Duniya a New York, aka sanar a ranar Alhamis.
Trump ya ce zai “fi son kar” ya kori Rosenstein amma dai an jinkirta haduwar ne dan kar a samu karo da sauraron kwamitin ‘yan majalisa na Shari’a wurin da Kavanaugh da wata matar da suke zargin shi da halayen da ba su dace ba akan jima’i, Dr Christine Blasey Ford, dukka sun bada shaida.
Ranar Juma’a, Trump ya bada umurnin binciken FBI na sti daya, akan ikirarai kan Kavanaugh, wanda ya kara kawo jinkiri ga zaben Yan Majalisa.
Sakataren Kakaki na Trump, Sara Saunders, ta bayyana a Fox News ranar Lahadi.
Da aka tambaye ta akan haduwar Rosenstein din, ta ce: “Ba’a saka rana ba ma wannan, zai iya zama wannan satin, ina ganin za’a iya masar da shi gaba da sati daya bisa ga dukka abubuwan da ke tafiya a babban kotun.
Amma za mu gani kuma za muci gaba da ‘yan jarida bayanai."
Wasu 'yan jarida za su yi hamayya da wannan bayani: Sanders bai gudanar da wani jawabi a Fadar White House tun 10 Satumba.
Mai watsa shiri Chris Wallace ya tambayi me yasa.
Sanders ya ce, rashin yin jawabin da aka yi bai kasance ba ne saboda matsala ga masu sauraro na TV, "duk da cewa ta ce: "Ba zan karyata gaskiyar ba cewa su na da kima."
Daga nan sai ta ba da shawarar ganinTrump kai tsaye hakan zai sa ‘yan jarida su karu.
"Shugaban ya yi karin Q & A zaman lafiya fiye da kowane shugaban da yake gabansa," inji ta, ba tare da nuna shaida ba: "Mun duba wadannan lambobin."
Jawabin zai gabata har yanzu, in ji Sanders, amma "idan manema labarai na da damar tambayar shugaban Amurka tambayoyin, kai tsaye toh yafi kyau fiye da magana da ni.
Mun yi ƙoƙarin yin haka sosai kuma kun gan mu yin hakan sosai a cikin 'yan makonnin da suka wuce kuma wannan zai faru na taƙaitaccen jawabi lokacin da za ku iya magana da shugaban Amurka."
Trump yakan amsa tambayoyi lokacin fita daga White House ko idan ya hallarci budaden taro ko taron manema labarai da baki masu ziyara.
Boyayen jawabin manema labarai na da wuya.
A Birnin New York wannan satin, shugaban kasa ya nuna dalilin da ya sa, ya ke yin ganin daman sa da kuma fitowa lokuta masu ban mamaki kafin ya tattara manema labarai.
Sakataren kiwon lafiya ya rubuta wa ma'aikatan EU a NHS Scotland game da tsoron Brexit
Sakataren Lafiya ya rubuta wa ma'aikatan EU da ke aikin NHS na Scotland don nuna godiya ga kasar kuma su na so su zauna bayan-Brexit.
Jeane Freeman MSP ta aika da wasika kasa da watanni shida don tafiya har sai Birtaniya ta janye daga EU.
Gwamnatin Scotland ta rigaya ta yi ƙoƙari don saduwa da farashin da za a bi don biyan bukatun 'yan ƙasa na EU waɗanda ke aiki a cikin ayyukan jama'a.
A cikin wasikar ta, Ms Freeman ta rubuta: "A lokacin rani, tattaunawar tsakanin Birtaniya da EU a kan janyewa ya ci gaba, zuwa ga yanke shawarar wannan kakan.
Amma Gwamnatin Birtaniya ta ci gaba da shirye-shirye don yiwuwar rashin daidaitawa.
Na san wannan lokaci dole yako rashin natsuwa gare ku duka.
Shi ya sa nake so in sake nuna yadda kowone ma’aikaci ke da daraja a gudummawar da yake bayarwa, ko dan wane ƙasa ne.
Abokan aiki daga ko'ina cikin EU, da kuma bayan haka, su na ba da kwarewa mai mahimmanci don ƙarfafawa da inganta aikin kiwon lafiya, da kuma amfani da marasa lafiya da al'ummomin da muke bautawa.
Scotland ta zama cikakken gida kuma munfi son ku zauna nan."
Anyi wa Christion Abercrombie Tiyatar Gaggawa Bayan Raunin da ya Samu a Kai
Tennessee State Tigers linebacker Christion Abercrombie aka wa tiyata gaggawa bayan raunin da ya ji a kai ranar Asabar da ta sha kashi 31-27 ga Vanderbilt Commodores, kamfanin Organic na Tennessean suka kawo rehoton.
Shugaban kocin Tennessee Rod Reed ya shaida wa manema labaru cewa raunin da ya faru ya faru ne kafin rabin lokaci.
Ya je daidai layin gefe kuma anan ya fadi”, Reed yace.
Masu horarwa da ma'aikatan kiwon lafiya sun ba Abercrombie oxygen a kan gefen layi kafin su sanya shi a kan shimfiɗa da kuma mayar da shi don ƙarin kimantawa.
Jami’in daga Jaha Tennessee ya fada wa Chris Harris na WSMV a Nashville,Tennessee, cewa Abercrobie ya fito daga tiyatar a Asibitin Vanderbilt.
Harris ya kara da cewa "babu cikakkun bayanai akan irin/yawan raunin tukunan" kuma Jihar Tennessee na kokarin gano lokacin da rauni ya faru.
Abercrombie, mai jar rigar sophomore,yana cikin kakar sa na farko tare da Jaha Tennessee bayan canja wuri daga Illinois.
Yana da tabi biyar a ranar Asabar kafin fita daga wasan, wanda ya kawo kakarsa har zuwa tabi 18.
Za a caje masu siya na ƙetare mafi girma aikin hatimi idan sun sayi dukiya a Birtaniya
Za a caje masu siya na ƙetare mafi girma aikin hatimi idan sun sayi dukiya a Birtaniya tare da karin tsabar kudi da ake amfani da su don taimaka wa marasa gida a karkashin sabon shirin Tory
Wannan motsi zai kawar da nasarar Corbyn don jawo hankalin matasa masu jefa kuri'a
Aikin hatimi zai yi tasiri a kan waɗanda ba su biyan haraji a Birtaniya
Ma’ajiyar kudin tsammanin tashin sa har zuwa miliyan £120 a kowace shekara - don taimaka wa marasa gida
Ana sa ran masu siyan na ƙetare za a caje su mafi girma aikin hatimi idan sun sayi dukiya a Birtaniya - tare da ƙarin tsabar kuɗin da ake amfani da su don taimaka wa marasa gida, Theresa May za ta sanar a yau.
Za a ga wannan matakin a matsayin ƙoƙarin kore nasarar da Jeremy Corbyn ya samu domin jawo hankalin matasa masu jefa kuri'a tare da alkawurra don samar da gidaje masu araha da kuma ƙaddara da samar da tsauraran matakai.
Aikin hatimin zai tashi ga akan daidaiku da kamfani da rashin biyan haraji a Birtaniya, tare da karin kudaden tallafawa gwamnatin ta hanyar magance rashin barci.
Ƙarin - wanda da yake kari ne ga aikin hatimi na yanzu, ciki har da matakan da aka gabatar a cikin shekaru biyu da suka gabata a kan gidaje biyu da kuma sayen bada haya - zai iya zama kusan kashi uku cikin dari.
Ma’ajiyar kudin na tsammanin tashin sa har zuwa miliyan £120 a shekara.
An kiyasta kimanin kashi 13 cikin dari na sababbin kayan haɗin gine-ginen London ana saye ne daga ‘yan kasar waje masu zama a Britaniya, farashin na hawa kuma yana sa masu sayen farko su wahala wajen samun gidajen shiga.
Yawancin yankuna masu arziki a kasar - musamman ma a babban birnin kasar - sun zama "biranen fatalwa" saboda yawan adadin masu saya na kasashen waje waɗanda mafi yawan lokutan basa zaune kasar.
Sabuwar manufofi ya zo ne kawai makonni bayan Boris Johnson ya yi kira ga takaddamar hatimi don taimakawa matasan da suka mallaki gidansu.
Ya zargi manyan Kamfanonin gine-gine da ajiye kayyaki masu manyan farashin ta hanyar karbe ƙasa ba tare da yin amfani da ita ba, kuma ya bukaci Mrs May ta bar kudaden shiga kan gidajen don magance "matsalar gidaje a Britaniya.”
Mista Corbyn ya sanar da wani tsari na gyaran gidaje da aka tsara, ciki har da tsarin haya da kuma kawo ƙarshen “rashin-lafin” fitarwa.
Har ila yau, yana so ya ba majalisa ikon da zai iya gina gidaje.
Mrs May tace: "A bara na ce zan keɓe mulki don maido da mafarkin Birtaniya - cewa rayuwa ta fi kyau ga kowane sabon ƙarni.
Kuma wannan yana nufin gyaran gidajen kasuwannin da suka rushe.
Birtaniya za ta kasance a bude ga mutanen da suke so su zauna, aiki da gina rayuwa a nan.
Duk da haka, ba daidai ba ne cewa yana da sauƙi ga mutanen da ba su zaune a Birtaniya, da kuma kamfanoni na kasashen waje, don sayen gidaje a matsayin mazaunan Birtaniya masu wahala.
Ga mutane da yawa mafarkin mallakar gida ya zama da nisa sosai, kuma rashin tausayi na mummunar barci yana kara tabbatuwa da gaske. "
Jack Ross: 'Babban burin na shi ne in gudanar da Scotland'
Shugaban Sunderland Jack Ross ya ce "burinsa" shi ne ya zama kocin Scotland a wani mataki.
Scot, mai shekaru 42, yana farin cikin kalubalantar dawoda kungiyar wasan na North-East, wanda a halin yanzu ke zama na uku a League na daya, maki uku daga saman.
Ya koma Stadium mai Haske a wannan kakar rani bayan ya jagoranci St Mirren komawa fremiya kakar wasan Scotland.
"Ina so in buga wa kasarta wasa.
Na samu hular B kuma wannan shi ne, "in ji Ross ya shaidawa BBC Scotland’s Muryarwasanni."
"Amma na girma da kallon Scotland a Hampden da yawa tare da mahaifina a matsayin yaro, kuma yana da wani abu ke jawoni.
Wannan damar za ta zo, duk da haka, idan na ci nasara a gudanar da kungiyar."
Wadanda suka gabaci Ross a matsayin masu gudarwa Sunderland sun hada da Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet da Paolo Di Canio.
Tsohon shugaban Alloa Athletic ya ce ba ya tsoron abin da wadannan sunayen suka kafa a irin wannan babban kungiyar, bayan da yaki tayin Barnsley da Ipswich Town.
"Nasara a gare ni a wannan lokacin shi ne 'zan iya mayar da kungiyar zuwa Wasanin Fremiya?'
Saboda tsari da kayayyaki a wannan kungiya, ba abun mamaki ba ne mu na Wassanin Fremiya, "in ji shi.
"Ba abu mai sauki ba ne don samun shi a can, amma zan iya ganin kai na kamar yadda na ci nasara a nan idan na iya samun kungiyar a can."
Shekaru Ross uku ne kawai a aikin gudanarwa, bayan wani lokaci a matsayin mataimakin mai gudanarwa a Dumbarton da kuma watanni 15 a Hearts 'koyon gudanar da wasanni.
Ya kuma taimakawa Alloa ta sake farfadowa zuwa rukuni na uku, kuma ya sake canza St Mirren daga rawar ta taka a gasar zakarun Turai a kakar wasa ta gaba.
Kuma Ross ya ce yana jin dadi fiye da yadda ya taba yi a lokacin da yake wasa a Clyde, Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren da Hamilton Academical.
"Ya zama mai yiyuwa da rudarwa," ya tuna, ya karbi ragamar Alloa.
"Na yi imani da gaske cewa gudanarwa ya fi dacewa da ni, fiye da wasa.
Yana da ban mamaki saboda na yi kokari, na yi rayuwa mai kyau daga ciki, kuma na ji dadin wasu daukaka.
Amma wasa zai iya zama da wuya.
Akwai abubuwa masu yawa da za ka fuskanta a kowane mako-mako.
Har yanzu ina ci gaba da wannan batun dangane da matsalolin da matsa lamba na aikin amma gudanarwa na ji daidai.
A koyaushe ina so in gudanar kuma yanzu ina yin hakan, ina jin dadi sosai da ina cikin kumbin a tsawon rayuwana."

Gudun zafi ya bunkasa shiga wajen shakatawa Birtaniya da ke fafatawa amma ya kara matsa lamba a kan gidajen cin abinci.
Wajajen shakatawa da mashaya sun samu tashin ciniki da kashi 2.7 bisa dari, a yuli amma wajajen cin abinci sun sauka da kashi 4.8 cikin dari, adadi sun nuna.
Peter Martin, mai kula da harkokin kasuwancin CGA, wanda ya hada da adadi, ya ce: "Ya ci gaba da haskakawa da Ingila fiye da yadda aka sa ran shiga cikin gasar cin kofin duniya a watan Yuli, wanda ya biyo bayan irin wannan yanayin zuwa watan Yuni na baya, a lokacin da aka samu kashi 2.8 cikin dari, sai dai yawancin gidajen cin abinci sun fi taɓuwa.
Faduwar kashi 1.8 cikin dari a cinikin sayar da abinci a watan Yuni kawai ya munana a watan Yuli.
Rumfunan saida abin sha da mashaya sun kara karfi tare da ire-iren sa fiye da gidajen cin abinci da suka kasance kasa.
Rumfunan sayar da abinci suma sun sha wahala a rana, amma bai kai ga irin na ma’ikatan gidajen cin abinci ba.
Da alama mutane su na so su fita ne don samun abun sha.
A duk wuraren da ake gudanar da shan giya da mashayar ababen sha sayarwa ya kai har 6.6 cikin dari na watan, da abinci kasa da kashi uku. "
Paul Newman, na manazartan shakatawa da karamcin RSM ya ce: "Wadannan sakamakon sun ci gaba da yayi tun daga karshen Afrilu.
Yanayi da kuma tasirin manyan abubuwan zamantakewar jama'a ko abubuwan dake faruwa a wasanni sun kasance manyan dalilai idan aka zo maganar sayarwa a kasuwar wajen gida.
Ba abin mamaki ba ne cewa kungiyoyin gidajen cin abinci na ci gaba da gwagwarmaya, don hana faduwar zuwa kashi 4.8 cikin dari a shekara domin zai kasance da tsananin ciwo a kan matsin lamba tsada da ake fuskanta.
Bazarar zafi mai tsawo ba zai iya zuwa a mafi munin lokaci ba ga masu sarrafa abinci kamar wannan ba kuma lokaci zai fada mafi matsakaicin yanayin da muka fuskanta a watan Agustan zai samar da jinkirin da ake bukata. "
Jimillar kudaden sayarwa a fadin wuraren shaye-shaye da gidajen cin abinci, wanda ya hada da budewa, ya kasance kashi 2.7 cikin watan Yuli, yana nuna jinkirin a fitarwar kamfanin.
Kamfanin Kasuwancin Coffer Peach Tracker na sa idanu ga kamfanonin Birtaniya, yankin mashaya da gidajen cin abinci da ke tattarawa da kuma nazarin tattalin bayanan da aka samu daga kungiyoyi masu aiki 47, da karuwar fiye da dala biliyan 9,kuma shi ne tushen alamar masana'antar.

Daya cikin yara biyar - wasu har yan shekara 11 - na da shafin yanar gizo na sirri da suke boyema iyayen su da malaman su, bincike ya nuna
Binciken yara yan sakandare 20,000 ya nuna karuwa a shafin “Insta na karya”
Labaren ya kara girmama tsoron cewa ana buga bayanan jima'i
Kashi ishirin na daliban sun ce su na da “ainihin” shafin da su ke nuna ma iyaye
Daya cikin yara biyar - wasu har yan shekara 11 - na kirkirar shafin yanar gizo da suke boyema manya.
Bincike a kan yara yan makaranta 20,000 ya nuna saurin karuwar shafukan “Insta na karya” - nassoshi da raba hotuna a shafin yanar-gizo na Instagram.
Labaren ya kara girmama tsoron cewa ana buga bayanan jima'i.
Kashi ishirin na yaran sun ce su na aiki da "ainihin" tsaftataccen shafin don nunawa iyaye, yayin da suke da na sirri.
Wata mahaifiyar da ta yi tuntuɓe da shafin yanar gizon 'yarta mai shekaru 13 na sirri ta sami wata matashiya tana roƙon wasu su "yi min fyade.”
Binciken, wayar da kan Dijital UK da shuwagabannin makarantu da shugabar makarantun taron (HMC) din makarantu masu zaman kansu, sun samu kashi 40 na yan shekara 11 zuwa 18 na da bayanai biyu, da rabin su na amincewa su na da shafuka na sirri.
HMC chief Mike Buchanan ya ce: “Abun damuwa ne matasa da yawa na sha’awar bude shafukan yanar gizo a inda iyaye da malaman su bazasu gano su ba.”

Tallar Nau’rar tatsar nono wanda ke kwatanta iyaye mata da shanu ya rarraba ra'ayi a kan yanar gizo
Wani kamfanin Nau’rar tatsar nono ya rarraba ra'ayi a kan yanar gizo da talla dake kwatanta na iyaye mata masu shayarwa da shanu ana tatsan su.
Don nuna kaddamar da abin da ake cewa shi ne "na’urar tatsar nono na sakawa a jiki na farko a duniya," kamfanin Elvie mai amfani da fasaha ya ba da tallan labaran kiɗa na launi don nuna 'yanci da sabon famfo ya bayar ga iyaye mata.

Daruruwan yara 'Yan gudun hijira sun tafi a hankali zuwa sansanin alfarma a kan iyakar Texas
Yawan adadin yara 'yan gudun hijirar da ake tsare da su sun karu ko da yake haɗin kan iyakoki a kowane wata ya kasance ba tare da canzawa ba, a wani bangare saboda rashin amincewa da manufofi da gwamnatin Trump ya gabatar da shi ya sa ya fi ƙarfin sanya yara tare da masu tallafawa.
A al'adance, yawancin masu tallafawa sun kasance baƙi ne ba tare da izini ba, kuma su na jin tsoro samun daman ikon kansu na kasancewa a cikin ƙasa ta hanyar ci gaba da bukata yara.
Haɗarin ya haɓaka a watan Yuni, lokacin da hukumomin tarayya suka bayyana cewa masu tallafawa da sauran 'yan ƙananan mazaunan su a gida zasu bada zanen hannun su, kuma za a raba bayanai tare da hukumomin shige da fice.

Daga bisani hukumar ta tabbatar da cewar kashi 70 cikin dari na waɗanda aka kama ba su da takardun laifi.
"Kusan kashi 80 cikin dari na mutanen da suke da goyon baya ko masu goyon baya na gida su na nan a cikin kasar ba tare da izini ba, kuma babban ɓangare na waɗanda su ne masu laifi.
Don haka mu na ci gaba da bin wadannan mutane, "in ji Mr. Albence.
Nema don aiwatar da yara da sauri, jami'ai sun gabatar da sababbin ka'idodin da zasu bukaci wasu daga cikinsu su bayyana a kotu a cikin wata daya da aka tsare, maimakon bayan kwanaki 60, wanda shi ne daidaitattun baya, bisa ga ma'aikatan tsari.
Mutane da yawa za su fito ta hanyar kiran taro na bidiyo, maimakon mutum, don yin jigilar su game da shari'a, a matsayin mai hukunci.
Waɗanda ake zaton ba su cancanci taimako ba za mu mayar da su.

Sham ta fada wa ‘sojojin mamaya’ na Amurka, Faransa da Turkiya zasu janye ba tare da jinkiri ba
A jawabi ma Majalisar Dinkin Duniya, Ministan Harkokin Waje al-Moualem yayi kira ga masu gudun hijira na da su dawo gida, duk da yakin kasar yanzu yana cikin shekara na takwas.
Moualem, wanda yake kuma matsayin mataimakin firayam minista, yace sojojin kasar wajen su na Sham ne ba tare da izini ba, a karkashin babatun yaki da ta’addanci, kuma “za’a magance su yadda ya kamata.”
“Dole su janye ba tare da jinkiri ba kuma ba tare da wani sharaɗi ba,” ya fada wa taron.
Moualem ya dage cewa “yaki da ta’addanci ya kusan karewa” a Sham, wurin da fiye da mutane 360,000 suka rasa rayuwar su tun 2011, tare da rashin gidajen miliyoyin mutane.
ya ce Damascus zata ci gaba da “yakin nan mai sarki har sai an tsarkake dukka yankunan Sham” na duk kungiyoyin ta’addanci da “duk wani jami’i da ke nan ba tare da izini ba.”
Amurka tana da wasu sojoji 2,000 a Sham, akasarinsu su na ba da horo da shawara wa sojojin Kurdawa da Larabawan Sham da basa son Shugaban kasar Bashar al-Assad.
Faransa tana da fiye da sojoji 1,000 a kasar da ke fama da yakin.
Akan batun yan gudun hijira, Moualem ya ce yanayin sun gyaru masu su dawo, kuma ya zargi “wasu ƙasashen yammaci” da “yada tsoro mara kyau” da yasa masu gudun hijira suka ƙi dawowa.
“Mun yi kira ga kasashen duniya da kungiyoyin agaji su sauƙaƙe da dawowar su,” ya ce.
“Su na siyasance abun da zallan batun jin kai ne.”
Amurka da Kungiyar Turai sun ba da gargadi cewa ba za’a bayar da agajin sake gine-ginen Sham ba har sai an samu yarjejeniya tsakanin Assad da ‘yan adawa ga yakin.
ma’aikatan hulɗa na Majalisar Dinkin Duniya sun ce wani yarjejeniya na kwanan nan tsakanin Rasha da Turkiya dan kebe tudun mun tsira a babban yankin karshe da ‘yan adawa suke rike da shi a Idlib ya samar da daman ci gaba da maganganun siyasa.
Yarjejeniyar Rasha da Turkiyar ya kawar da babban hari da ‘yan Sham masu goyon bayan Rasha suka kai lardin, wurin da mutane miliyan uku suke zama.
Moualem duk da haka ya jadadda cewa yarjejeniyar ta na da “bayyanannen kwanaki” kuma sun bayyana sa rai cewa aikin sojoji zai mayar da hankali ga ‘yan ta’adda ne tare da mafaɗa daga Nusra Front masu alaka da Al-Qaeda, waɗanda “za’a magance.”
Wakilin Majalisar Ɗinkin Duniya Staffan de Mistura yana sa ran cikin kwanan nan zai kira taron farko na kwamitin wanda ke kunsheda mambobin gwamnati da na ‘yan adawa su rubuta tsarin mulkin kasa bayan yaki na Sham ya kuma buɗe hanyar zabe.
Moualem ya fitar da sharruɗan da zasu sa gwamnatin Sham ta shiga cikin kwamitin, yana cewa a kuntata aikin bangarorin “zuwa yin bitar dokokin wannan tsarin mulkin na yau,” kuma yana bada gargaɗin tsangwama.

Kuɗin waje ya cika mafi kusancin zaben tsakiyar wa’adi na ‘yan majalisa
Ba abun mamaki bane cewa 17 na Pennsylvania yana ganin kuɗi masu yawa, godiya ga sake daidaituwar gundumar majalisa da ya kawo ga masu sarauta biyu a gasar kujera ɗaya.
Wannan sabon tsarin yankunan wajen Pittsburg ya haɗda Ɗan Majalisar Jam’iyyar Damokraɗiya Conor Lamb - wanda ya ci kujerar a wata gundumar a wani zaben musamman bazarar da ta wuce.
Lamb yana takarar tare da wani Ɗan Majalisa, Ɗan jam’iyar Republican Keith Rothfus, wanda ke wakiltar tsohon Gundumar Pennsylvania na 12, wanda ya haɗda sosai da sabon na 17.
An sake zane taswirar ne bayan Babban Kotun Pennsylvania ta yanken hukunci a Janairu cewa an haɗe iyakan tsofaffin gundumomin na ba akan shari’a ba dan a yima jam’iyar Republicans ni’ima.
Takarar a sabon na 17 ɗin ya buɗe hanyar gasar kuɗi tsakanin saasan kuɗaɗen manyan jam’iyu, Kwamitin Yakin Zaben Majalisa na Damokraɗiya (DCCC) da Kwamitin Yakin Zaben na Kasa na Republicans (NRCC).
Lamb ya zama sanannen suna a Pennsylvania bayan matsatten nasara a wani zaben mussamman da aka kalla sosai a Maris na Majalisar 18 na Gundumar Pennsylvania.
Wannan kujerar da tana hannun Republican ne fiye da shekaru goma, kuma shugaban kasa Donald Trump ya ci gundumar da maki 20.
Manazartan siyasa sun ba wa jam’iyar Ɗamokraɗiya ɗan matsatsen sa’ar nasara.
Amurka Ta yi Nazarin Hukunta El Salvador Don Goyon Bayan China, Sai ta Fasa
Ma’aikatan hulɗa sun lura cewa Jamhuriryar Dominican da Panama sun riga sun shaida da Beijing, tare da ɗan karamin turi daga Washington.
Mr. Trump ya yi taron fara’a da Shugaba Juan Carlos Varela na Panama a Yuni 2017 kuma yana da otel a Panama har sai da abokanan sana’a suka kori masu gudanar da aikin kungiyar Trump.
Jami’an Sassan Kasa sun yanke hukunci su dawo da manyan ma’aikatan hulɗar Amurka da ke El Salvador, Jamhuriyar Dominacan da Panama akan wannan “hukuncin kwanan nan na daina shaida Taiwan,” Heather Nauert, kakakin sashen, ta faɗa a bayani farkon wannan watan.
Amma kawai tara aka yi nazari akan El Salvador, waɗanda suka samu kimanin agajin dala miliyan 140 daga Amurka a 2017, harda kula da kwayoyi, goyon bayan ci gaba da tattalin arziki.
Taran da aka yi nazarin, wanda har da yanke agajin kuɗi da kuntatawar takardun izinin shiga, da za su yi zafi wa Kasar ta Tsakiyar Amurka da ke fama da rashin aiki da kashe-kashe.
A yayin da taron cikin gidan ke guduna, Jami'ai na Arewacin Amurka da na tsakiya sun dakatar da wani taro mai zurfi kan batun tsaro da wadataccen tattalin arziki don bitan wannan taron na bara wanda aka ganshi a matsayin matakin kokarin hana masu gudun hijirar zuwa Amurka.
Amma a tsakiyar watan Satumba, manyan jami'an gwamnati sun bayyana cewa su na so taron ya ci gaba, yadda ya kamata a kawo karshen hukuncin da ake yi wa El Salvador.
Mataimakin shugaban kasar Mike Pence yanzu an tsara zai yi bayani a taron, wanda aka shirya a tsakiyar watan Oktoba, a wata alama ta shigo da ayyukan gwamnati a taron, in ji jakadan.
Kuma wakilan Amurka guda uku sun koma El Salvador, Panama da Jamhuriyar Dominica ba tare da sababbin saƙonni ko azabtarwa daga Washington ba.
Kakakin Fadar White House Mr. Bolton ya ƙi yin sharhi game da cikakken muhawarar da jami'an Amurka uku suka bayyana, ciki harda ma'aikatan diplomasiyya guda biyu, waɗanda suka amince da su tattauna boye a ciki.
an tabbatar da bayanansu daga manazarci wanda ke kusa da gwamnati kuma yayi magana a yanayin boye.
Karanta Tarihi

idan har majilisar ta chanza hannu, Mr. Trump zai samu kanshi cikin tuhumar daukar alhakin a wannan gamayyar, kamar yadda yake shirin komawa gaban masu zabe, kuma kila ta kasance a tsakanin sa’oin shi.

Rangers' Graham Dorrans yana da yakini gabanin haduwar Rapid Vienna
Rangers sun karbi bakuncin Rapid Vienna a ranar Alhamis, inda suka san cewa nasarar da ta samu a kan Austrians, bayan zira kwallo a Spain da Villarreal a farkon wannan watan, zai sanya su cikin matsayi mai karfi don samun damar shiga kungiyar G na Europa League.
Raunin gwiwa ya hana dan wasan tsakiya Graham Dorrans buga farkon kakar wasa ta bana har zuwa 2-2 da Villarreal amma ya yi imanin cewa Rangers zai iya amfani da wannan sakamakon a matsayin matashi zuwa ga manyan abubuwa.
"Wannan maki ne mai kyau a gare mu saboda Villarreal na da kyau," a cewar dan shekaru 31.

Mata na kasa barci saboda tsoron rasa kudin ajiyarsu na ritaya
Duk da cewa mahalarta binciken su na da ra'ayi game da yadda suke so a kula da su, kadan daga cikin mutane su na magana da' yan uwansu game da shi.
Kusan rabin mutane a nazarin duk kasar sun ce su na magana da matansu game da kudin da ake kulawa da dadewa.
Kashi 10 bisa dari ne kawai sukayi magana da yayan su game da haka.
"Mutane su na son dangi su kula da su, amma ba su daukan matakai don tattaunawa," in ji Holly Snyder, Mataimakin Shugaban Hukumar Harkokin inshura.
Ga inda za a fara.
Kayi ma matar ka magana da yaran: Bazaka iya shirya iyalin ka don samun kulawa ba idan baka bayyanar da fatan ka an sani ba kafin lokaci.
Kayi aiki da masu baka shawara da iyalin ka don tattauna ina da yanda za’a karbi kulawa, don wadannan zabubbukan nada muhimman abubuwa don kayyade kudin.
Shigo da mai bada shawara akan harkokin kudin ka: Mai baka shawara na iya taimaka maka ne wajen nuna maka hanyoyin da zaka iya biyan wadancan kudin da aka kashe.
Zaɓen kuɗin daukar nauyin ka na kulawar dogon zangona iya haɗawa da manufofin inshora na kula da dogon zango na gargajiya, wani matashin manufofin inshoran muhimmancin kudi don taimakawa wajen rufe wadancan kudaden da aka kashe ko inshoran kai da kudin ka -matukar kanada kudin.
Fito da takaddun shari’ar ka: Kashe fadace-fadace na doka a lokacin baya.
Nemi wani wakili na kiwon lafiya a wurin domin ka zaɓi mutumin da ka amincema don kula da lafiyar ya kuma tabbatar da cewa kwararru sunbi bukatun ka koda ka kasa magana.
Har ila yau, kayi la'akari da ikon lauya don kudaden ka.
Zaka zabi mutum daya da ka yarda da shi don yanke shawara game da kudaden ka da kuma tabbatar da an biya cajin kudade koda bazaka iya biya ba.

An harbe mutum sau da yawa da bindigar iska a Ilfracombe
An harbi wani mutum sau da yawa da bindigar iska yayin da yake tafiya gida daga fitar dare.
Wanda aka harban, yana cikin shekarunsa na 40, yana yankin Oxford Grove din llfracombe, Devon, a yayin da aka harbe shi a kirji, cibiya da hannu.
Jami’an sun bayyana harbin, wanda ya gudana da misalin 02:30 BST, a matsayin “mai aukuwa akai-akai.”
Wanda aka harban baiga wanda ya harbe shi ba.
Raunukan shi ba masu barazana ga rayuwa bane kuma yan sanda na rokon shaidu su fito.
Girgizar kasa da tsunamis a Indonesia
Akalla mutane 384 ne suka rasa rayukansu sakamakon wani girgizar kasa da tsunami mai tsanani da suka faru a birnin Palu ranar Juma’a, Jami'an suka ce, ana sa ran karuwar waɗanda suka mutu.
Saboda rashin hanyar sadarwa, jami'an tsaro ba su samu kowane bayani daga Donggala regency ba, wani yanki a arewacin Palu wanda ya fi kusa da farfadowar girgizar kasa mai karfin 7.5.
A Palu, an kwashe mutane fiye da 16,000 bayan da bala'in ya fara.
Ga wadansu bayanai game da Palu da Donggala, akan tsibirin Sulawesi:
Palu shi ne babban birnin lardin Sulawesi na tsakiya, wanda yake a ƙarshen bakin teku a yammacin bakin tekun tsibirin Sulawesi, tare da kimanin mutane 379,800 a 2017.
Birnin yana bikin tunawa da shekaru 40 a lokacin da girgizar kasa da tsunami suka fara.
Donggala wani tsari ne wanda ke tafiya fiye da kilomita 300 (kilomita 180) na bakin teku a arewa maso yammacin tsibirin Sulawesi.
Tsarin mulki, wani yanki na kasa da ke ƙasa a lardin, nada kimanin mutane 299,200 a shekarar 2017.
su da aikin noma sune ainihin yanayin tattalin arzikin lardin Sulawesi, musamman ma yankunan bakin teku na Donggala.
Nickel mining ma yana da mahimmanci a lardin, amma mafi yawa ya fi mayar da hankali ne a Morowali, a gefen kudancin Sulawesi.
Paman da Donggala sun sha samun aukuwar tsunamis a cikin shekaru 100 da suka gabata, in ji kamfanin Indonesia's Disaster Mitigation.
A 1938, tsunami ya kashe mutane fiye da 200 kuma ya hallaka daruruwan gidaje a Donggala.
Wani tsunami kuma ya bugi yammacin Donggala a shekarar 1996, ya kashe mutane tara.
Indonesia na zaune a kan tsaunuka na Pacific Ring na Wuta kuma girgizar kasa na yawan samunsu.
Ga wasu manyan girgizar ƙasa da tsunami a cikin 'yan shekarun nan:
2004: Babban girgizar kasa a yammacin tekun Aceh dake arewacin Sumatra a ranar 26 ga Disamban bara ya haifar da tsunami wanda ya shafi kasashe 14, inda ya kashe mutane 226,000 a bakin tekun Indiya, fiye da rabin su a Aceh.
2005: Jerin girgizar kasa ya faru a yammacin tsibirin Sumatra a cikin karshen Maris da farkon Afrilu.
Daruruwa sun mutu a tsibirin Nias, a bakin tekun Sumatra.
2006: Girman 6.8 auku a kudancin Java, tsibirin da yafi kowanne cika a Indonesia, wanda ya haifar da tsunami wanda ya shiga har kudancin bakin teku, inda ya kashe kusan mutane 700.
2009: Girgizar kasa mai girma ta 7.6 ta auku a kusa da birnin Padang, babban birnin lardin yammacin Sumatra.
Fiye da mutane 1,100 aka kashe.
2010: Girgizar kasa mai girma ta 7.5 ta auku a daya daga cikin tsibirin Mentawai, daga Sumatra, inda ta haifar da tsunami har zuwa mita 10 da suka lalata kananan garuruwa masu yawa kuma suka kashe kimanin mutane 300.
2016: Wani mummunan girgizar kasa ya auku a yankin Pidie Jaya a Aceh, ya haddasa rugurgujewar abubuwa da tsoro yayin da aka tunatar da mutane game da mummunan girgizar kasa da tsunami da ta auku a 2004.
Ba a sami tsunami ba a wannan lokaci, amma fiye da mutane 100 suka mutu sakamakon gine-ginen da suka fadi.
2018: Babban girgizar kasar ya auku a tsibirin Lombok dake Indonesiya, inda ya kashe mutane sama da 500, mafi yawa a arewacin tsibirin.
Girgizar ta ruguza dubban gine-gine kuma ta bar dubban masu 'yan yawon bude ido cikin wani hali na dan lokaci.
An kama babban dan Sarah Palin kan tuhumar rikicin cikin gida
Track Palin, babban dan tsohon gwanan Alaska kuma mataimakin shugaban dan takara Sarah Palin, an kama shi kan tuhumar cin zarafi.
An kama Palin, mai shekaru 29, na Wasilla, Alaska, kan zargin da ake yi na tada hankalin cikin gida, tare da yin katsalandan ga rahotannin tada hankali cikin gida da, a cewar wani rahoton da Alaska State Troopers ta fitar, a ranar Asabar.
A cewar rahoton 'yan sanda, idan wata mata tayi kokarin ta kira' yan sanda don bayar da rahoton laifukan da ake zargin, sai ya dauki wayarta daga gareta
An sa Palin a cikin Mat-Su Pretrial Facility kuma ana gudanar da shi a kan yarjejeniyar takardar alkawali na $500, in ji KTUU.
Ya bayyana a kotu a ranar Asabar, inda ya bayyana kansa "ba laifi ba, a gaskiya" lokacin da aka neme shi, ruwaitowar cibiyar sadarwa.
Palin yana fuskantar nau'o'i uku na Aji na, ma'ana zai iya tsare shi har zuwa shekara guda kuma ya biya $ 250,000.
Ana kuma tuhuma shi da wani mummunan lakabi na Ajin B, wanda hukunci shi ne ya je kurkuku na rana guda da kuma tarar $2,000.
Ba shi ne karo na farko da aka gurfanar da Palin ba akan mayan laifuka.
A watan Disamba na shekara ta 2017, an zarge shi da kisa ga mahaifinsa, Todd Palin.
Mahaifiyarsa, Sarah Palin, ta kira 'yan sanda don bayar da rahoto game da harin.
Shari’ar tana gaban Kotun Tsohon Kotun Alaska a yanzu haka.
A watan Janairu 2016 an zargi shi da aikata laifuka na gida, da rikici da rahoto game da aikata ta'addanci a cikin gida, da kuma samun makamin yayin da yake cike da haɗari dangane da wannan lamarin.
Budurwar shi ta yi zargin cewa ya doke ta a fuska.
An soki Sarah Palin a lamarin ta hanyar kungiyoyin tsofaffin soja a shekara ta 2016 bayan ya haɗu da halayyar danginta ga PTSD daga aikinsa a Iraki.
Girgizar kasar Indonesia ta tsunami: daruruwa sun mutu
Akalla mutane 384 ne suka mutu bayan girgizar kasa ta mamaye tsibirin Sulawesi a Indonesia a ranar Juma’a.
Girgizar kasa mai magnitude 7.5 ya haifar da tsunami kuma ya rushe dubban gidajen.
Harkokin lantarki da sadarwar sun lalace tare da tsammani karin matattu za' tashi a cikin kwanaki masu zuwa.
Girgizar ta fara ne kawai daga tsakiyar Sulawesi wanda ke arewa maso gabashin kasar Indonesia, Jakarta.
Bidio na ta yawu a shafukan watsa labarai na nuna lokacin tasiri.
Daruruwan mutane sun taru don bikin rairayin bakin teku a birnin Palu lokacin da tsunami ya rushe a bakin tekun.
Masu gabatar da kara na tarayya na neman hukuncin kisa na kisa ga dan ta’adda NYC
Masu gabatar da kara na tarayya a birnin New York suna neman hukuncin kisa ga Sayfullo Saipov, wanda ake zargin a harin da ya faru a birnin New York, wanda ya kashe mutane takwas - hukuncin da ba a yi ba a jihar don aikata laifukan tarayya tun shekara ta 1953.
Saipov, mai shekaru 30, ya yi amfani da motoci mai hawa na gida domin gudanar da hare-haren kan hanyar machine da ta hanyar West Side Highway a Lower Manhattan, inda ya kaddamar akan masu tafiya a kafa da kekuna a hanyarsa a watan Oktoba.
Don tabbatar da hukuncin kisa, masu gabatar da kara za su tabbatar da cewa Saipov "da gangan" ya kashe mutane takwas da "ganganci" ya jawo mummunan rauni a jiki, bisa ga sanarwar na neman hukuncin kisa, aka a yankin Kudancin Sabon Gundumar New York.
Dukkan waɗanda nan la'akari su na da hukuncin kisa, bisa ga takardun kotu.
Makonni bayan harin, babban kotun tarayya ta maka wa Saipov zarge-zarge 22 da suka hada da laifuffuka guda takwas na kisan kai don taimakon rashin gaskiya, yawanci sune masu gabatar da kara ke yi a laifukan shiryeyyen laifi, da kuma cajin tashin hankali da halakar da motoci.
Wannan harin ya bukaci "tsarawa mai mahimmanci da kaddamarwa," in ji masu gabatar da kara, inda ya bayyana irin yadda Saipov ya dauki shi a matsayin "mai mugunta, mummunan hali da kuma marar sa tausayi."
"Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov ya haifar da rauni, cuta, da hasara ga iyalai da abokai Diego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza, da Alejandro Damian Pagnucco," sanarwa na niyyar jihohi.
Biyar daga cikin waɗanda aka kashe 'yan yawon bude ido daga Argentina
An yi shekaru goma tun lokacin da yankin kudancin New York ya kaddamar da hukuncin kisa.
Wanda aka gurfanar da shi, Khalid Barnes, an yanke masa hukunci ne game da kashe masu raba kwaya biyu, amma an yanke masa hukuncin kisa a watan Satumba na 2009.
karshen a lokacin da aka yanke hukuncin kisa a tarayya New York a 1953 ga Julius da Ethel Rosenberg, ma'aurata bayan da aka yanke musu hukuncin kulla makirci don Tarayyar Soviet a lokacin Yakin Tsana shekaru biyu da suka gabata.
Dukansu Rosenbergs sun mutu ne ta hanyar kujerar lantarki ranar 19 ga Yuni, 1953.
Saipov, dan kasar Uzbekistan, ya nuna rashin tausayi a cikin kwanaki da watanni bayan harin, bisa ga takardun kotu.
Ya bayyana wa masu binciken cewa ya jin daɗin abin da ya yi, 'yan sanda sun ce.
Saipov ya shaida wa hukumomin da cewa ya samu kwarin guiwa bayan gudanar da harin bayan ya duba bidiyon ISIS a wayarsa, bisa ga zargin.
Har ila yau, ya bukaci a nuna tutar Isis a cikin dakin asibiti, in ji 'yan sanda.
Ya yi zargin ba shi da laifi ga tuhuma 22 na zargin.
David Patton, daya daga cikin masu kare hakkin jama'a na tarayya a jihar Saipov, ya ce su na da "takaici" tare da yanke shawara.
"Mu na tsammanin shawarar da za a nemi hukuncin kisa maimakon karɓar laifin mai laifi zuwa rai a kurkuku ba tare da yiwuwar saki ba zai shawo kan matsalolin abubuwan da ke faruwa ga kowa da kowa", inji Patton.
Lauyoyi masu kare Saipov sun nemi masu gabatar da kara kada su nemi hukuncin kisa.
Tory MP ya ce NIGEL FARAGE ya kamata a kula da tattaunawar Brexit
Nigel Farage ya yi alwashin yin 'yan tawaye a yau yayin zanga-zanga a taron Tory.
Tsohon shugaban Ukip ya ce 'yan siyasar sun' ji zafi 'daga' yan kasuwa na Eurosceptics - kamar yadda daya daga cikin wakilai na Theresa May ta ba da shawara cewa ya kamata tayi la'akari da tattaunawar da EU.
Wani mai goyon baya na baya-bayan nan, Peter Bone, ya shaida wa manema labaru a Birmingham cewa Birtaniya za ta fita daga yanzu idan Mr Farage ya zama Sakatare Brexit.
Amma ƙalubalen da Mrs May ta fuskanta wajen sulhu da ragamar da aka yi a tsakanin bangarori daban-daban da aka yi sun nuna cewa, Pro-Remain Tories na shiga cikin rashin amincewa da Brexit a birnin.
Fremiya na fama da matsalolin kulawa da masu bincikenta sunyi shiri akan hanya a cikin hare-hare daga Brexiteers, Remainers da EU.
Abokai sun dage cewa ta tura gaba tare da ƙoƙarina buga yarjejeniyar tare da Brussels duk da sakamakon - kuma ta tilasta yan Turai da Labour don su zabi tsakaninta da 'rudani'.
Mista Bone ya shaida wa kamfanin dillancin labaran AFP cewa, yana son 'duba' 'Masu binciken'.
Ya ba da shawarar cewa Mr Farage ya kamata ya zama dan takara kuma ya ba da alhakin tattaunawar da Brussels.
"In da ya kasance mai kula, da yanzu mun fita," in ji shi.
The Wellingborough MP ya kara: 'Zan tsaya a kan Brexit amma mu na buƙatar mu duba masu bincike.'
Da yake nuna adawa da EU, ya ce: 'Ba mu yi yaƙe-yaƙe na duniya ba don mu zama kaskantattu.
Mu na son yin dokokinmu a ƙasar mu.’'
Mr Bone ya yi watsi da cewa shawarwarin da ra'ayoyin jama'a sun canja tun lokacin zaben 2016: 'Da ra'ayin cewa mutanen Birtaniya sun canza tunaninsu kuma su na so su kasance ba daidai ba ne.'
Tory Brexiteer Andrea Jenkyns ya kasance a cikin tafiyar, yana mai ba da rahotanni: ‘Ina cewa kawai: Frem minister ya saurari mutane.
'Masu bincike ba su da tsaurin ra'ayi tare da jama'a, da' Yan adawa ba za su yi zabe ba, ba tare da jam'iyyarmu da 'yan gwagwarmayarmu ba, waɗanda suka lalata tituna kuma suka sa mu zaɓa tun a farkon.
Don Allah sauke Masu bincike kuma ka fara sauraro.'
A cikin sakon da aka nuna wa Mrs May, ta kara da cewa: 'Firaim Ministocin su na ci gaba da aikin su idan sun kiyaye alkawuransu.'
Mr Farage ya fadawa 'yan siyasa cewa dole ne' yan siyasar su fara 'jin zafi' idan su na son cin yaudara da aka yi a cikin referendum na 2016.

Kungiyar Dundee Stars sun dau fansar rashin da sukayi ga Elite League a kan Belfast Giants ta hanyar lashe gasar 5-3 a Dundee ranar Asabar.

Amma duk da abokan aikin sa sun gudu don tserar da rayukansu, Anthonius Gunawan Agung, mai shekaru 21, ya ki ya bar gurin aikin sa a gini hasumiya a filin jirgin saman Maniara Sis Al Jufri dake filin jirgin saman Palu.

Lambobin masu murabus a Koriya ta Arewa ya'sauka' a karkashin Kim
Yawan mutanen Arewacin Koriya masu murabus zuwa Korea ta Kudu ya sauka tun lokacin da Kim Jong-un ya hau mulki a cikin shekaru bakwai da suka gabata, wani mai kula da ka'idoji na Koriya ta kudu ya ce.
Park Byeong-seug, wanda ya bada bayanai daga ma'aikatar hadin kai ta Kudu, ya ce an samu raguwar murabus 1,127 a bara - idan aka kwatanta da 2,706 a shekarar 2011.
Mr Park ya ce, karin tsaron kan iyakan da ke tsakanin Koriya ta Arewa da Sin da kuma karin yawan farashin da masu fasa kwari ke yi sun kasance manyan dalilai.
Pyongyang bai yi wani bayani ba a baya ne.
Mafi yawan masu murabus daga Arewa su na samun kyautar zama dan kasar Koriya ta kudu.
Seoul ya ce fiye da mutane 30,000 Arewa Koreans sun ketare iyaka ta hanyar haramtacciyar hanya tun lokacin karshen yakin Koriya a 1953.
Yawancin mutane sun tsere daga kasar Sin, wanda ke da dogon iyakaci da Koriya ta Arewa kuma ya fi sauƙin ketarewa fiye da yankin (DMZ) dake da kwakwaran tsaro a tsakanin Korear biyu.
Kasar Sin ta na la'akari da masu murabus a matsayin masu shigowa ba bisa ka’ida ba a maimakon 'yan gudun hijira dan haka su na mai da su.
Harkokin dangantaka a Arewa da Kudu - waɗanda har yanzu su na yaki - sun inganta a cikin 'yan watanni.
Tun a farko wannan watan, shugabannin kasashen biyu sun gana a Pyongyang don tattaunawar da suka danganci tattaunawar sulhun rusa makaman nukiliya.
Wannan ya zo bayan taron kafa tarihi Yuni tsakanin shugaban Amurka Donald Trump da Kim Jong-un a Singapore, lokacin da suka amince da yarjejeniyar da za ta kai ga raba kasar da makaman nukiliya.
Bayan taron Yuni tsakanin shugaban Amurka Donald Trump da Kim Jong-un a Singapore, sun amince da su shiga yarjejeniya don amfani da Jamhuriyyar Arewa maso gabashin Congo.
Ya ce, "Ba tare da amincewa da Amurka ba, ba za mu amince da tsaron lafiyarmu ba, kuma a irin wadannan yanayi, babu wata hanyar da za lalata makaman mu da kanmu," in ji Mr Ri a cikin jawabinsa ga Majalisar Dinkin Duniya a birnin New York.

Yadda yakin kasuwancin Amurka-Sin zai iya zama alheri ga Beijing
Makusudin fara yakin kasuwancin a tsakanin Amurka da Sin masu karfi ne, kuma matsala ba mai tsayawa yanzu bane, a tsakanin kasashen biyu kuma zai iya zama alheri ga Beijing na tsawon lokaci, in ji masana.
Donald Trump, shugaban kasar Amurka, yayi gargadin farko a farkon wannan shekarar ta hanyar sanya haraji kayayyakin fitarwa muhimmnai na kasar Sin, ciki har da feifen sola, karfe da dalma.
Babban haɓakar da aka yi a wannan makon tare jadawalin kuɗin fito da suka shafi dala biliyan 200 (£150 biliyan) kimanin kayan, ta yadda za a biya kashi ɗaya daga cikin kayayyaki da ke zuwa Amurka daga kasar Sin.
Beijing ta rama duk acikin nau'i daya, cikin kwanan nan sun kara jadawalin kuɗin fito daga kashi biyar zuwa kashi goma a cikin dala biliyan 60 na kayan Amurka.
Kasar Sin sunyi alkawarin amfani da tsarin Amurka na harbe ni-in harbe ka, kuma kasar wace itace to biyu a duniyan tatalin arziki ba su shirya jenyewa ba nan kusa.
Sanya Washington to janye kuma yana nufin kumawa cikin nema, amma janye wa Amurka a bainar jama’a zai fi zama abun kunya ga Xi Jinping, Shugaban Kasar Sin.
Duk da haka, masana sun ce idan Beijing za ta iya buga katunansa daidai, Amurka za ta iya tallafawa kasar Sin cikin dogon lokaci ta hanyar rage- dogaro na tattalin arziki.
"Gaskiya cewa a yanke shawarar siyasa cikin sauri a Washington ko Beijing zai iya haifar da yanayin da zai rage tattalin arziki a kowace kasa ya zama mafi haɗari fiye da yadda masu kallo suka amince a gabanin haka," in ji Abigail Grace, wani mai bincike da ke kula da Asiya. Cibiyar Sabon Tsaro ta Amurka, mai tankin tunanin.
Siriya ta “shirya” don dawo da 'yan gudun hijira, in ji ministan harkokin waje
Siriya tace ashirye take su karbi yan gudun hijira da suka sa kansu dawowa kuma su na rokon neman taimakon sake gina kasar da ya ruguje sakamakon yakin da dauki fiye da shekara bakwai.
Da suke magana da Babbar Majalisar Dinki Duniya, ministan harkokin waje Walid al-Moualem yace yanayin kasar na kara inganta.
Ya ce, "Yau halin da ake ciki a cikin ƙasa ya kasance mafi karko da kuma tabbatar da godiya ga cigaban da aka samu wajen yaki da ta'addanci," inji shi.
Gwamnati ta ci gaba da sake gyara wuraren da 'yan ta'adda suka ruguza don dawo da zaman lafiya.
Dukkan yanayi sun kasance yanzu don dawo da 'yan gudun hijirar zuwa kasar sun fita ne saboda ta'addanci da kuma matakan tattalin arziki da suka shafi rayuwarsu ta yau da kullum da muhallin su.
Majalisar Dinkin Duniya ta kiyasta cewa fiye da mutane miliyan 5.5 sun tsere daga kasar tun lokacin da aka fara yakin shekarar 2011.
Wasu mutane miliyan shida da ke zaune a kasar su na bukatar taimakon agaji.
Al-Moualem ya ce gwamnatin Siriya za ta maraba da taimako wajen sake gina ƙasar da aka rushe.
Amma, ya jaddada cewa, ba zai yarda da tallafi ba, ko taimako daga kasashen da suka tallafa wa tashin hankalin.
Turai taci gasar kofin Ryder a Paris
Kungiyar Turai ta lashe gasar cin kofin Ryder Cup da cin kungiyar Amurka a wasan karshe na 2018 wasan ya kammalla da maki 16.5 zuwa 10.5 a Le Golf National waje Paris, Faransa.
A yanzu haka Amurka ta rasa sau shida a jere akan kasar Turai kuma ba ta lashe kofin Ryder a Turai tun 1993.
Turai ta sake komawa kambi da dan wasan Denmark kyaftin Thomas Bjorn wanda ya kai maki 14.5 da suke buƙata na doke Amurka.
Fitaccen jarumi Amurka Phil Mickelson, wanda ya ka attaka komai a wasan, ya jefa kwallo a cikin ruwa a par-3 rami na 16, inda ya barwa Francesco Molinari wasan shi.
Golfer Molinari na Italiya ya haskaka a cikin dukan raga, ya zama dan wasa 1-daga-4 da za su ci gaba da ci 5-0-0 tun lokacin da aka fara gasar a shekarar 1979.
Dan wasan Amurka Jordan Spieth ya fita akan 5&4 daga cikin 'yan wasa mafi ƙasƙanci a tawagar Turai, Thorbjorn Olesen na Denmark.
Dustin Johnson, dan wasan gaba na duniya, ya fadi ne 2 da 1 zuwa Ian Poulter na Ingila wanda ya taka leda a gasar cin kofin Ryder na karshe.
Tsohon dan wasa gasar Ryder na takwas, Serbia Garcia ya zama dan wasan da ya lashe gasar cin kofin Turai a kowane lokaci da maki 25.5.

Ingancin Jan Igiyar Ruwa Sinadarai na raguwa a Pinellas, Manatee da Sarasota
Sababbin rahotanni daga Hukumar Florida Fish da wildlife na nuna raguwar sinadaran Jar Igiyar Ruwa a sassan yankin Tampa Bay.
A cewar FWC,ana samun rahoton yanayin tsagewar kyalli bayar a yankunan Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Charlotte da Collier - wanda yake nuna rage yawan sinadarai.
Kyallin Jar Igiyar Ruwa na kara yaduwa kimanin kilomita 130 na coastline daga kasashen arewacin Pinellas zuwa kudancin Lee.
Ana iya samun tsagewa kimanin kilomita 10 daga bakin takun kasar Hillsborough, amma a yankuna kadan da suke da alaka da makon da ya gabata
An kuma lura da Jar Igiyar Ruwa a kasar Pasco.
An bayar da rahoton samuwar sinadarai matsakaita a bakin teku da ke kasar Pinellas a cikin makon da ya gabata, ƙananan zuwa mafi girman sinadai a bakin tekun a kasar Hillsborough, baya zuwa mafi girman sindarai a cikin ko bakin teku a kasar Manatee, baya zuwa gagarumin sindarai a cikin ko bakin tekun yammacin kasar Sarasota, baya zuwa matsakaicin sinadarai a kasar Charlotte, baya zuwa babban sinadarai a ciki ko bakin tekun na kasar Lee, da kuma ƙananan sinadarai a kasar Collier.
An cigaba da samun rahoton Raunin numfashi a kasashen Pinellas, Manatee, Lee, da Collier.
Ba a ruwaito raunin numfashi ba a Northwest Florida a cikin makon da ya gabata.
